¶scala perfectionis capla prime partis ¶here begynnen chapytours present volume walter hylton namyd laten scala perfeccionis englysshed ladder perfeccōn whiche volume deuyded two partyes fyrst boke present volume conteyneth l • xxxiii chapitours seconde boke xlvi whiche hole volume amonuteth cxxxix chapitours ¶that inner 〈◊〉 mane soule sholde belyke vtter capitulū primum actyff lyfe werkes therof capitulū ii contēplatyfflyfe werkes therof caplm̄ iii fyrst part contemplacōn caplm̄ iiii seconde part contemplacōn caplm̄ v lower degree yt ii part contēplacōn ca vi hyer degree ii part cōtemplcōn ca vii thyrde part contemplacyon ca viii twynnynge thyrde part cōtemplacōn frothe seconde part praysynge therof ca ix shewynge bodyly wyttes felynge may bothe good euyll caplm̄ x ye shalte knowe whan shewynge ye bodely wyttes felynge ben good euyl ca xi knytteth iesu mannes soule losyth seth hym therfro caplm̄ xii thȳges contemplatyff man sholde occupyed capitulum xiii reason wyl vertue begynneth loue lykynge made perfyte capitulum xiiii ye meanes yt bryngeth soule cōtēplacōn ca xv man sholde vse refuse vertu mekenes ca xvi ¶who sholde blame mennes •• fawtes demehem caplm̄ xvii men sholde worshyp lowe hemself owne hert vnder al capitulum xviii men sholde wantyth felynge mekenes affeccōn dredyng moche therfore ca xix ypocrytes heretykes wantynge mekenes hyghen hemself hert al ca xx thīges mē owē byleue siker fayth ca xxi stable entent nedeful thyse sholde pleyse god dyscrecōn bodely werkes ca xxii lytyl rehersynge thynges sayd makynge offerynge ye sholde offeryd god ca xxiii prayer yt spedeful gete clennes hert vertu ca xxiiii men sholde pray wheron poynt thought shalbe sette prayer ca xxv fyre loue ca xxvi certayne prayer speche ordeyned god holy chyrche best hem y• ben new corned god deuocyon ca xxvii peryl men yt begynnynge tournynge god euen comyn prayer ordenaunce holy chyrche gyue hem medytacyon ca xxviii seconde maner prayer speche certaynly folowyth styrynge deuocyon ca xxix seconde maner prayer plesyth moche god makyth mā haue hym • ody drō ken makyth hym soule wounded swerde loue ca xxx tyre loue wasteth flesshly lustes fyre wasteth al bodely thynge ca xxxi thyrde maner prayer oonly ye hert without speche outwarde ca xxxii men sholde doo y• ben trauayled vayn thou ghtys prayer ca xxxiii ¶of meditacyon synfull men ben holy tourued god caplm̄ xxxiiii meditacōn manhede cryst hys passyon yeuen frely ye holy ghost shal knowen whan yeuen caplm̄ xxxv meditacōn ye passyō cryst withdrawē fro hem yeuen oft sythes dyues cause capitulum xxxvi dyuers temptacōns fende ca xxxvii dyuers remedyes ayenst temptacōns fende capitulum xxxviii god hem chesyth suffereth taryed tempted afterwarde • ō forteth hem stableth hem soule myghtes therof reke downe grounde • ynne therin ca xlii man shal knowe worthynes worshyp hys soule yt fyrst god wrechydnesse myscheue fal synne ca xliii ¶how euery man may saued ye passyon cryst neuer wretchyd capitulum xliiii mā sholde besye recouer ayen worthynes refourme ayē hȳ ye ymage ye trinyte ca xlv ihū shal sought desyred founde ca xlvi profyte haue ye desyre ihū ca xlvii thyng trauayle ghostly derknes ayenste ymage synne capitulum liiii propirly thymage syn̄e comyth therof capitulum lv pryde whan synne caplm̄ lvi whan pryde dedely synne flesshly lyuynge men dedely synne capitulum lvii pryde ypocrytes dedely synne ca lviii pryde heretykes dedely synne ca lix styrynges pryde vaynglory good men ben venyalsynnes capitulum lx dyuers state holy chyrche shall haue dyuers medes heuē two specyal medes heuē ca lxi short styrynge mekenes charyte ca lxii man shall knowe moche pryde hym capitulum lxiii enuye yre braunches stede synne mannys persone oft hated capitulū heretyke cursyd man capitulum lxvii good dede may make men saaf without charyte ye charyte fele yt bē meke ca lxviii man shall wyte moche wrathe enuye hydde grounde herte ca lxix token thou shal knowe yf thou louest thyn enmye ensample thou shal take cryst loue hym capitulum lxx man shal know moche couetise hidde hert capitulum lxxi man shal knowe whan synneth etynge dynkynge whan synneth hūger bodely paynes lettē moche ghostly werkynge capitulum lxxv remedye man shal vse ayenst defawte made •• ynge drynkynge capitulum lxxvi thorough besye desyre trauayle mekenes charyte man cometh sooner vertues trauayle hemselfe capitulum lxxvii derkenes ymage synne comyth wyndowes therof caplm̄ lxxviii soule defawte knowynge gooth ye v wyttes seche outwarde lykyng ca lxxix soule sholde begge capitulum primū ghostly suster ihesu cryst pray yt ye callynge whiche lorde hath callyd yt seruyce thou holde payd stondested fastly therin trauaylynge besely wyth al ye myghtes thy soule ye grace ihū cryst fulfyl sothfastnes good lyuynge ye state whyche thou haste take lyknes semyng thou hast forsake worlde dede man turned lorde bodely syght men ryght yt thyn hert myght dede al erthly loues dredes turned holy lorde ihū cryst wyte thou wel bodely tournynge god without hert folowynge fygure lyknes vertues noo sothfastnes wherfore wretched man woman leuyth inwardly kepynge hymself shapeth hȳ wythout forth oonly forme liknes holynes habyte clothynge speche bodely werkes beholdynge mennes dedes demynge defawces wenynge hymself ought whan right begyleth hymself thou turne thy hert thy body pryncipally god shape lycknes mekenes charyte ghostly vertues then̄e art thou truly torned hym say thou soo lyghtly fyrst day maye tournyd thy soule fulhede vertues thou myghte thy body closyd hous thou sholde knowe cause thy bodely closynge yt thou myght beter come ghostly closynge thy body closyd fro bodely conuersacōn men ryght thyn hert myght enclosed fro flesshly loues dredes al ecthly thynges thou myghte ye beter come therto shal tel lytyl wrytynge thynkyth ¶of actyflyf werkes therof caplm ii thou shate vnderstōde holy chyrche two maner lyues saynt gregory faythgreg y• whiche cristen sholde sauf one called actyf contēplat yf without one thyse ii noo man may sauyd actyflyflyeth loue charite shewed outwarde good bodely werkes ī fulfyllynge goddes cōmaundementes vii werkes mercy bodely ghostly man̄es euyn crysten lyf longeth worldly men whiche haue rychesse plēty worldly goodes spende al whiche haue state offyce cure men haue goodes spende lerid lewde temporel spirytuel generally al wordly men bounde fulfylle myght cūnynge reson discrecōn asketh moche good haue moche good doo lytyl haue lesse may doo yf nought haue thēne must haue good wyl thyse ben werkes actyflyf bodely ghostly also grete part actyflyflyeth grete bodely dedes whiche man doth hymself grete fastynge moche wakynge sharpe penaūce doynge chastyse flesshe wyth dyscrecōn trespace done suche penaunce refrayne lustes lykynges make hym buxū redy wyl spyryte thyse werkes though bē actyf helpe ryght moche ordeneth man begynnynge come cōtemplatyflyf yf bē vsed dyscrecyon ¶of contēplatyflyf werkes therof caplm iii contēplatyflyflyeth perfyte loue charyte felyd īwardly ghostli vertues fothfast knowynge syght god ghostly thynges lyflongeth hem specyally whiche loue god forsaketh al wordly rychesse worshyppes outwarde besynes hooly yeuen hem body soule myght cunnynge seruyse god ghostly ocupacōn thenne syth soo thy state asketh contēplatyf thētent thy enclosynge thou myght frely enteerly yeue ghostly ocupacōn thenne behouyth ryght besye nyght daye traueyle body spyrite come lyf nygh thou mayst suche meanes thou hopest best neuertheles telle meanes shal telle tyrst lytyl lyf contēplatyf thou might somwhat se sythen set marke ī syght thy soule wherto thou shalt drawe al thyn occupacyon ¶of fyrst part coutemplacyon caplm iiii contemplatyflyf hath thre partes fyrst lieth knowynge god ghostly thynges geten reason techyng man studye holy wryt without ghostly affeccōn inly sauour felyd ye specyal yefte holy ghost parte haue specyally lettred men grete clerkes whiche lōge studye trauaylle holy wrytte comen knowynge lesse ye subtylte kyndly wyt cōtynuaūce studye general wyt yt god yeueth euery man yt hath vse reason knowynge good maye called part contēplacōn asmoche syght sothfastnes knowynge ghostly thȳges neue •• theles fygure shadowe contēplac •• hath ghostly sauour god ne inwardly swetnes whiche man may fele yf ī grete charyte proper welle lorde whiche cometh none alien maner knowynge comyn good vadde maye without charyte therfore contēplacōn oft sithes ypocrytes flesshly lyuyng men haue suche knowynge many crystē men yet haue thyse men charyte maner knowynge spykyth saynt poul thꝰ si habuero oēm scienciā cor 13 nouerim misteria oīa caritatē aucē nō habeā nihil sū ful knowing al thynges knew al preuytees charyte y• haue cūnyng turneth pryde vaynglory hēself couetyse desyrynge worldly state worshyps ryches mekely takyng praysyng god ne charytably spēdeth ye ꝓfyte euēstrysten hē fallē heresyes errours ¶how men sholde pray wheron poynt thought shal set prayer caplm̄ xxv desyrest thou perauēture knowe thou sholdest pray vpon thynge thou sholde set poynt thy thought thy prayer also prayer best ye vse fyrst answere saye thus whan thou art wakenyd thy slepe redy pray thou shalte fele thyself flesshly heuy euer doūwarde vayne thoughtis dremes fātasyes vnskylful besynes worlde thy flesshe behoueth quycken thyn hert prayer styre moche thou may deuocyon thy prayer thou set thyn hert ony bodely thynge al thy traueyle shall drawe thought fro beholdynge al bodely thynge thy desyre myght nakyd bare fro al erthly thynges euer vpwarde styenge vnto ihesu cryst thou may neuer see bydely godhede ne bodely lyknes ymaginacyon thou may chrugh deuoute contynuel beholdynge mekenes precyous manhede fele thy say haue sayd ¶that certē prayer speche ordened god holy chyrche best hē y• bē new tourned god deuocyō ca xxvii knowe prayer best vse shal say thynke thou shalt vnderstonde yt ben iii maner prayer fyrst prayer speche made specyally god pater noster made also generally thordynaunce holy chyrche matyns euensonge houres also made deuoute men specyal sayenges lorde lady sayntes maner prayer whiche callyd vocal thynketh vnto art relygyous custome rule art bounde say mateyns houres holde moost spedeful say hem deuoutly thou mayst whan thou sayest thy mateyns thou sayest also thy pater noster pryncypally styre deuocyon ordened say also psalmes ympnes suche whiche bē made holy ghost pater noster therfore thou shalt say hem hastely rechelesly thou euyl apayd thou art bounde hem thou shalt gader thyn affeccyon thy thought say hem sadly deuoutly ony othrer specyall prayer deuocyon trowynge forsothe syth prayer holy chyrche ther prayer profytable whiche vocal vse comynly shall thou put away al heuanes grace thou shalt turne thy nede good wyll thy bonde grete fredom yt shal lettynge ghostly ocupacyō thou may yf thou wyll vse thy pater noster ony suche thise whiche thou felest see wretchydnes thy soule mynde somtyme stablyd god ryght hath forgoten hym sekith rest creature one nother neuer may fynde ful reste hath loste hym ful reste ryght soo reason loue also whiche clene ghostly sauour swetnes tournyd fowle bestly lust lykynge self creature flesshly sauours wyttes gloteny lechery ymagynyng ī pryde vaynglory couetise somoche thou mayst vnnethes ony good dede yf thou defoyled vaynglory ne thou maye wel vse none thy v wyttes clenly creature delectable yf thy herte taken e • gleymed veyne lust lykynge whiche putteth loue god fro hert felynge ghostly sauour may come therin euery mā lyueth spyryte knowith wel al wretchydnes soule myscheyf fyrst synne man without al wretchydnes synnes whiche thou hast wylfully put therto wyte thou well though thou neuer done synne thy body dedely ne venyal oonly called orygynal fyrst synne elles lesynge thy ryghtfulnes whiche thou made ī sholde thou neuer haue ben saued yf lorde ihū cryste precyous passyon delyuerde restored ye ayen ¶how euery man may saued ye passyon cryst neuer wretched caplm̄ xliiii therfore yf thou thynke haue spoken hye thou mayst take ne fulfylle haue sayd shal say wyl fal downe lowe thou wyl profyte wel thyn thenne say thus though thou neuer somoche wretche haue thou doo neuer somoche synne forsake thyself thy werkes good bad crye mercy aske on̄ •• saluacyō vertue precyous passyō mekely trustly without dout thou shal haue oryginal syn al thou shalt saaf ye thou shal saaf anker incluse oonly thou al crystē soules whiche trustē vpō passiō meken hēself knowlegyng wretchydnes askyng mercy foryeuenes ye fruyt precyous passyō lowyng hēself sacramentes holy chyrche though beso yt haue ben encōbred synne al lyftyme ne • er felynge ghostly • auour swetnes ghostly knowyng god ghostly seke man lyueth withoute synne whiche ghostly syknes saynt iohn̄ sayth hymselfe perfyte men thus si dixerimus qr pccm̄ non habemusioh ip̄i no ceduci mu e • veritas nobis non est saye haue synne begyle ourself sothfastnes v therfore maye neuer come ioy heuen vnto fyrst made hole ghostly sykenes ghostly hele may man haue hath vse reason yf desyre loue haue delyte therin ī moche hopyth gete ye name ihū nothynge elles ghostly hele wherfore soth yt say may man saaf yf loue lyke name ihesu may man ghostly hole yf loue desyre ghostly helth ryght yf man bodely seke erthly thynge dere ne nedful hym ne moche sholde desyred hym bodely helth though thou woldest yeue hym al rychesse worshyppes worlde make hym hole thou myghte thou plesest hym right soo man seke ghostly felyth ye payne ghostly syknes thynge dere ne nedefull ne moche coueyted hym ghostly helth ihesu without whiche al ioyes heuen may lyke hȳ thys skylle hope lorde whā toke mankynde saluacyon wolde called name betokenyd endles beyng wysdom ryghtwysnes oonly ye betokenyd cause comynge saluacyon mannes soule whiche saluacyon betokened name ihesu then̄e semyth soth shall man saaf yf loue saluacyon oonly haue thrugh mercy lorde ihesu merytes passyon whiche loue may haue lyuyth deyeth lowest degree charyte also maye saye partye loue thys blessyd name ihū gostly myrth ne encrease ī heuēly melodie shal neuer haue ne fele ī heuē ye fulhede souereyne ioye whiche myght lyf aboundaunce perfyte charyte ihesu shal fele haue maye sayenge vnderstonde neuertheles shal faaf haue ful mede syght god yf lyf ye lowest degre chartte kepynge goddis commauudementes lorde sayth hymself thus modo patris mei mansiones multisunt faders hous many soundry dwellynges perfyte soules ye whiche lyfe fulfylled charyteiōh grace holy ghost songe louynges god contemplacyon hym wonderful swetnes heuenly sauour thyse soules moost charyte grace holy ghost shal haue hyest mede blysse heuen thise arn called goddis derlynge soules dysposyd contemplacyon god ne fulhede charyte apostle marters begyn̄ynge holy chyrche shal haue lower mede blysse heuen thyse arne called goddis frendes thus calleth lorde holy wrytte chosen soules sayenge thuscant comedite amici▪ et inebriamini carissimi frendes ete ye derlynges ye dronken yf lorde sayde thus ye arne frendes ye kept cōmaū dementes sette loue loue worlde loued ony erthly thynge ye shall fed wyth ghostly fode brede lyf ye yt arne frendes ye oonly kept cōmaūdementes also owne free wyll fulfylled counceylles ouer ye loued oonly enterly wyth al myghtes soule al maner syn̄es seuē ryuers whiche arne thyse pryde enuye ire accidie couetyse glotenye lecherie lo somwhat yt thou may fele one thyse ryuers ren̄eth al maner syn putteth charyte yf dedely syn̄e thyselfe whiche sheweth thy syght thy soule excellence ouerpassynge mē wymmen styryng thou felyst loue delyte vayne plesyng thy self thou art token thou berest blacke ymage whiche yf preue men̄es entente wrytynge ¶ neded mankynde yt oonly thorough ye passyō cryste sholde restored refourmed ye shape fyrste synne caplm ii ryghtwysnes god sketh yt trespace done foryeuen yf amendes made yf may done sooth mankynde yt hole adam fyrste man trespassed agaynste god wonder greuously whan forfeyted ye specyal byddynge hym assented false counsayle fende deserued ryghtfully haue departed fro hym dampned helle withouten ende ferforth stondynge ryghtwysnes god myght foryeuen yf amendes fyrste made full satysfaccyon therfore amendes myght man make man oonly comen adā kyndely generacyon skylle trespasse vnworshyp endles grete therfore passyd mā ny myght make amēdes also skyl yt hath trespassed shal make amendes hym behouyth yeue hym yt hath trespassed vnto al owyth though trespassed also ouer hym behouyth yeue sōwhat owyth oonly trespassed mankynde myght paye god trespaas ouer ought hym gode dede man myght body soule dette euery man ought gospel sayth loue god al herte al soule myghtes better myght neuertheles dede suffyced refourmynge mankynde ne myght yf fyrst refourmed thenne neded yf mannes soule sholde refourmed ye trespaas made gode lorde god hymself sholde refourme ymage make amendes trespaas sythen man myght myght godhede myght ne ought make amendes sufferyng payne owne kynde therfore neded sholde take mankynde trespassed become man myght comyn lawe generacyon impossyble goddis sonne borne towchyd woman therfore hym muste become man thoroughe gracyous generacyon werkynge ye holy ghoste clene gracious mayden lady saynt mary done lorde ihesu goddes sonne became mā thorugh precyous deth suffred made amendes ye fader heuē man̄es gylte ye myght well god oughte hymselfe moche man borne ye kynde yt adam fyrst trespaced though ought owne persone hymself myghte synne neuertheles oughte free wyll trespaas mankynde whiche mankynde toke saluacyon man endeles mercy soth neuer man myght yelde god ony thynge owne ought oonly blessyd ihesu myght paye god one thynge ought hymselfe nought one thynge yeue precyous lyfe wylful takyng dethe loue sothfastnes ought moche good myght y• worshyp god lyfe al dette take dethe loue ryghtwysnesse bounde therto bounde ryghtwysnesse boonde deye dethe oonly payne ordeyned man owne synne lorde ihesu synned neuer ne might synne therfore ought deye thenne sythen ought deye▪ yet wylfully deyed thenne payde god thā ought sythen beste mannes dede moost worthy euer done therfore resonable synne mankynde sholde foryeuen moche mankynde founde mā ye kynde without wemme synne ihesu myght make amendes trespaas done myght paye lorde god al ought ouer yt ought syth lorde ihesu god man deyed thus saluacyon mannes soule ryghtful yt syn sholde foryeuen man̄es soule yt ymage sholde mow reformed restored fyrst lyknes ye blysse heuen passyon lorde precyous dethe grounde al ye refourmyng al mannes soule without whiche myght neuer mannes soule haue refourmed lyckenesse hym ne come blysse heuen blessyd may al werkynge thorough vertue precyous passyon brennyng swerde cherubyn droue adam paradyce put awaye ye endles gate heuen arn open euery man wyl entre therto persone ihesu bothe god kynge heuen blysse fader man porter yt yate redy receyue euery soule yt wyl refourmed ī lyf lycknes may euery soule yf yt wyl refourmed ye lykenesse god syth yt trespaas yeuen amendes thorugh ihesu made fyrste gylte neuertheles though sothe al soules haue profyte ne frute nf precyous passyon ne arne refourmed ye lyckenes hym iewes paynyms also fals crysten men bē refourmed effectually thorough vertue ye passyon owne defawte caplm iii two manere men arne refourmed vertue passyon one hem yt trowe hē yt loue iewes paynems haue benefyce passyon trowe iewes trow yt ihū sone ye vyrgyn mary goddys sone heuen also paynems trowe yt souereyne wysdome god wolde become son man manhede wolde suffre paynes deth therfore iewes helde prechynge ye crosse passyon cryste nought sclaunder blasphemye paynems helde nought fantome folye true crysten men helde souereyne wysdom god grete myghte thus sayd saynt poul predicamus vobis crystū crucifixum iude quidam scandelū gentibus autem stulticiam ip̄is autē vocatis iudeis grecis xp̄m dei virtutem et dei sapienciam co rum preche ye trowe ihesu cryst crucyfyed son mary goddis son scuereyne vertue wysdom god whiche ihesu iewes paynems trowe hym put sclaunder foly therfore thyse men vntrouthe putten hemselfe fro refourmynge owne soule stondynge vntrouthe shal neuer saaf ne come blysse heuen sothe fro begynnynge ye worlde vnto laste endyng neuer mā saaf ne shal • aaf yf trouth generall specyall ihesu cryste come come ryght al chosen soules incarnacyon vnder ye olde testamente hadden trouthe cryste sholde come refourme mannes soule eyther openly patryarkes prophetes holy men hadde elles pryuely generaly chyldern symple inperfyte soules hadden knewe specyally pryuyte incarnacyon ryght chosen soules vnder newe testamente hathe trouthe cryste come eyther openly felyngly ghostly men wyse men haue elles generally chyldern haue dyen crystned symple lewde soules haue arne nourysshed bosom holy chirche syth sothe thynketh thyse mē gretly greuously erren sayen iewes sarasyns kepynge owne lawe may made saaf though trowen ihū cryste holy chyrche trowyth moche wene y• owne trouth good syker suffysaunt saluacōn trouthe done semyth many gode dedes ryghtwysnes perauenture yf knewe crysten fayth better owne wolde leue owne take therfore yt sholde saaf naye ynough soo cryste god man bothe waye ende medyatour betwene god man withoute hym maye soule reconsyled ne come blysse heuen therfore trowen hym god man maye neuer saaf ne come blysse men also louen cryste passyon arne refourmed soule lyckenes hym thyse men arne false crysten men whiche arne oute charyte lyuen deyen dedely synne thyse men trowen wel semyth ihesu goddis son passyon suffyseth saluacōn mannes soule trowe also artycles faythe vushaply trouthe dede loue hym ne chese frute passyon lyen stylle synne false loue worlde vnto laste ende ben refonrmed lyckenesse god goon paynes helle endelesly iewes sarasyns done moche gretter payne moche ye trouthe kepte trespaas neuer hadde thenne yf thou wolte wyte whiche soules arne refourmed lyfe ymage god thoroughe vertue passyon soothly oonly trowen hym louen hym whiche soules ymage god thorough synne forshapen fowle bestes lyckenes restored refourmed ye fyrst shape worthynes worshyp begynnynge withoute whiche restorynge refourmynge shall neuer soule faaf ne come blysse two maner refourmynges ymage one ī fulnes another fayth caplm iiii sayest thou maye soth ymage god whiche mannes soule myghte refourmyd lyfe lyckenesse ony creature semyth naye myght yf refourmed sholde haue stable mynde clere syght clere brennynge loue god ghostly thynges euerlastyngly begynnyng yt creature thou trowest lyuynge lyfe ayenst thyself thou canst wel saye thynke ful ferre therfro thy mynde thy reason ye loue thy soule arne moche sette beholdyng ī loue erthly thynges ghostly thynges thou felyst ryght lytyl thou felyst refourmynge thyselfe thou arte vnbylapped blacke ymage synne ought yt thou maye vpon syde thou tour ne thou felyst thyself defoyled spotted flesshly styrynges foule ymage chaūgyng felyst thou none fro flesshlynes ghostlynesse neyther pryue myghtes thy soule ne bodely felynge wherfore ye thynken myghte yt ymage myght refourmed elles yf myght refourmed thenne askest thou myght refourmed answere laye thus two manere refourmyng ymage god whiche mannes soule one fulnesse nother partye refourmynge fulnesse maye lyfe delayed lyfe ye blys • e heuen mannes soule shal fully refourmed state fyrste begynnyng kynde myght haue thorough grace yf stonde hole shal restored moche blysse moche hyer ioye thorough grete mercy endles goodnesse god shold haue yf neuer fallen shal soule receyue hole ye ful felyng god al mightes without medelyng ony affeccyon shal see mankynde persone ihesu aboue ye kynde angel onyd godhede shal ihū bothe god man al al oonly heisay • none ye prophete sayth dominus solus exaltabitur illa die lorde ihesu daye yt euerlastyng daye shal hyghed oonly none also ye body man shal gloryfyed shall receyue fully ryche dowary vndedelynes al yt longeth therto shal soule haue ye body moche saye shall blysse heuen lyfe though yt passyō lorde cause al ful refourmynge mannes soule soules salu • cyō whiche nomber fulfylled tyme passyon therfore neded length tyme thorough kyndly generyon men sholde fulfylled thenne yf sone dethe lorde euery soule wolde haue trowed hym sholde lyfe haue blessyd ful refourmed without ony abydynge wolde creature lyued thenne haue ne wolde haue receyued ye faythe haue made blessyd thenne sholde generacyon haue ceased sholde arne chosen souled lyuynge soules come v haue ben borne sholde lorde haue fayles nomber maye therfore lorde purueyed moche better v delayed full refourmyng mannes soule tyl laste ende saynt poul sayth deo pro nobis melius prouidentedē br ne siue nobis consūmarentur lorde purueyeth better v delaye refourmynge yf graunted thenne skylle chosen soules beforne sholde make ful ende without v come nother skylle syth another refourmynge ymage partye refourmynge maye lyfe yf lyfe maye neuer ne soule may neuer saaf refourmynge two maners one fayth oonly nother fayth felynge fyrst refourmynge fayth oonly suffyseth saluacyon seconde worthy haue passynge mede blysse heuen fyrst maye hadde lyghtly shorte tyme seconde maye soo thoroughe lengthe tyme moche ghostly traueyle fyrste maye hadde felynge ymage synne thoughe man fele noo thynge hymselfe styrynges synne flesshly desyres ayenstondynge felynge yf wylfully assent therto maye refourmed fayth lyckenesse god seconde refourmynge puttyth lykynge felynge flesshly styrynges worldly desyres suffreth noo suche spottes abyde ymage fyrste refourmynge oonly begyn • ynge profytynge soules actyfmen seconde perfyte soules contemplatyfmen fyrste refourmynge ymage synne destroyed lefte hole felynge seconde refourmynge destroyeth olde felynges ymage synne bryngeth soule newe gracyous felynges thoroughe werkynge holy ghoste fyrste good seconde better thyrde blysse heuen moost beste fyrste lette v speke one sythe soo shall come thyrde thorough sacrament baptym yt grounded passyon cryst ymage refourmed fro orygynal synne caplm̄ vi two manere synnes makyth • le lese ye shape lyknesse god one called orygynal yt ye fyrst syn thother called actuel yt wylfully done syn thise ii syn̄es put away soule fro ye blysse heuē dāpneth thēdles payn hel thorough grace god refourmyd lyckenesse passe hen lyfe neuertheles two remedyes arne ayenst thyse two synnes yt whiche forshapen soule maye restored agayne one ye sacramente baptym ayenste orygynal synne nother sacramente penaunce ayenst actuel syn̄e soule chylde borne vncrystenyd cause orygynal synne hath lyckenesse god nought ymage fende bronde helle soone crystened refourmed ymage god thorugh vertue fayth holy chyrche sodeynly tourned fro lyckenesse ye fende made lyke angel heuen also ye falleth iewe sarazyne whiche ben crystened arne nought mancyples helle whan forsaken errour fallen heuen withoute ony lettyng done neuer moche synne tyme vntrouthe neuer sholde fele paynes helle ne purgatory ye pryuelege sholde haue meryte crystis passyon thorough sacrament penaunce ye stondeth contrycyon confessyon satysfaccyon ymage refourmed fro actual synne caplm̄ vii also crysten man woman yt hath lost ye lyckenesse god thoroughe dedely synne brekynge goddis commaundementes yf thoroughe wchynge grace sothfastly forsake synne sorowe contricyon herte ful wyl amende hym torne hym good lyuynge forsayd wyl receyueth sacramente penaunce yf maye yf maye wyltherto sothly saye mannes soule woman yt forshapen fyrste lyknesse deuyl thorough dedely synne nowe sacrament penaunce restored shapen ayen ymage lorde god grete curtesye lorde endles mercy lyghtly foryeuyth al maner synne soo sodeynly yeuyth plente grace synful soule askyth mercy hym abydeth grete penaunce doynge ne paynful flesshly sufferyng foryeue askyth lothynge synne ful forsakynge wyl soule loue hym tournyng ye hert hym askyth yeuyth then̄e whan seeth withoute ony delayenge foryeuyth synne refourmyth soule lyknesse synne foryeuen soule shal dampned neuerthelesse payne detted synne yet fully foryeuen yf contrycyon loue therfore shal go shewe hym shriue hym ghostly rader receyue penaūce enioyned trespaas gladly fulfyl bothe synne ye payne maye done awaye passe hen skylful ordynaunce holy chyrche grete profyte mannes soule thoughe synne foryeuen thorough vertue contrycyon neuerthelesse fulfyllynge mekenesse make hole satysfaccyon shal yf may shewe preste plener confessyō yt token warraunt foryeuenesse ayenste al enmyes yt nedefull haue yf man forfeyted lyfe ayenst kyng erthe ynough hym fulsykernesse haue on̄ly foryeuenesse kynge yf haue charter whiche may token warraunt agaynste al men ryght maye sayd ghostly man haue forfeyted agaynst kynge heuen lyfe thorough dedely synne ynough hym fulsykernesse haue foryeuenes god oonly contrycyon betwene god hym yf haue charter made holy chyrche yf maye come therto sacrament penaunce whiche charter token foryeuenes syth forfeyted ayenste god holy chyrche skylful haue foryeuenesse one warrant ye oo skylle confession nedeful nother skylle syth refourmyng soule stondyth fayth oonly felyng therfore flesshly man rude boystouse deme lyghtly outwarde bodely thynges sholde mow haue crowyd yt synnes ben foryeuē hym yf bodely token confessyon thorough whiche token made • syker foryeuenes yf yt hym trouth holy chyrche vnderstonde also nother skylle though grounde foryeuenesse stonde pryncypally confessyon contrycyon ye herte forthyn kynge synne neuertheles hope many soule sholde neuer felyd contricyō full forsakynge synne yf confessyon fallyth oft sythes tyme coufessyon grace compunccyon comyth soule neuer felyd grace euer colde drye ferder fro felyng grace therfore syth confessyon profytable partye crysten men holy chyrche ordeyned sykernesse generally al crystē men euery man woman sholde one yere lest shryuen synnes come mynde ghostly fader though neuer soo moche contrycyon tyme neuertheles hope wel yf al men ben besye aboute kepyng themselfe eschewynge almaner synne comyn moche grete knowynge felyng god man hathe holy chyrche sholde haue ordeyned token confessyon nedeful bonde neded al men arne perfyte perauenture moche partye crysten men vnperfyte therfore holy chyrche ordeyned confessyon waye general bonde al crysten men wyl knowe holy chyrche moder wol buxome byddynge soth hope erreth gretely generally sayth confessyon synnes shewe preste neyther nedeful synner ne behoful man bounde therto haue sayd
