vnperceyuable worchynge holy ghost ymage refourmed though seen ne felt calpm̄ viii refourmange stondeth fayth felyng ryght propyrte fayth trowe yt thou seest ryght trowe ye thou felyst yt refourmed soule ye sacrament penaunce ye ymage god felyth chaūgynge hymself neyther bodely kynde without ne pryue substaunce soule within dyde vnto felynge felyth styrynges synne corrupcyon flesshe passyons worldly rysynge herte dyde neuertheles shal trowe yt thorugh grace refourmed ye lyknes god though nother fele ne see may wel fele sorowe synne tornyng wyll fro syn̄e clēnesse lyuynge yf yt haue grace take good kepe hymselfe may nother see ne fele refourmyng soule wonderly vnperceyuably chaunged fro ye fylthe fende vnto fayrnes angel thorough pryue gracyous werchyng holy ghost maye see shal trowe yf trowe soule refourmed trouthe ryght holy chyrche trowith ye sacrament baptym sothfastly receyued iewe sarasyn chylde borne refourmed soule lyckenesse god thorough pryue vnperceyuable werthyng holy ghost ayē stōdyng al ye flesshly styrynges body syn ye whiche shal fele baptim wel dyde ryght ye sacrament penaūce mekely truly recōmaundement god thou haste mysdone ayenste byddyng thou hast shryuen y• therof mekely ful herte leue arte sory thou dydest saye sykerly thy soule refourmed fayth lyknes god ¶that al soules lyuen mekely faythe holy chyrche haue fayth quyckened loue chary ben refourmed sacrament though soo ye may fele y• specyal yefte deuocōn ghostly felynge calpm̄ x refourmynge oonly fayth ye moste parte chosen soules leden lyfe settē wyl stedfastly flee al manere dedely synne kepe hem loue charyte euen crystē kepe cōmaūdementes god cū nynge whan wycked styrynges euyl wylles rysen hertes pryde enuye yre lecherye ony hede synne ayenstonde hē stryuen ayenst hem dysplesyng wyl soo folowe dede thyse wycked wylles neuertheles yf falle lyghtly ayenst wyl thorugh freelte vncūnynge soone conscyence greuyth hem pynyth hem soo greuously mowe haue noo reste tyll shryuen maye haue foryeuenesse sothly al thyse soules thus lyuenin refourmynge ben founde therin houre dethe shall saaf come full refourmynge blysse heuen thoughe soo myghte neuer haue ghostly felynge ne inwarde sauoure ne specyall grace deuocyon al lyfe tyme elles yf thou saye noo soule shall • aaf refourmed ghostly felyng myght fele deuocyon ghostly sauour god soules doon thorough specyal grace sholde fewe soules saaf rewarde multytude nay trowe ye soules oonly arne deuoute grace come ghostly felynge mo lorde ihū sholde haue take mākynde suffred ye harde passyon dethe lytyl purchaas hym haue come fro ferre nere fro soo hye lowe fewe soules nay mercy spred larger soo neuertheles contrary wyse yf thou trowe yt passyon lorde soo precyous mercy moche yt shal soule dampned namely crysten man neuer euyll fooles wene sothly thou e • rest gretly therfore go ye meane holde ye myddes trowe holy chyrche trowith moost synful man yt lyueth yf torne wyl thorough grace fro dedely synne sothfaste repentaunce seruyce god refourmed soule yf deyed ye state shal saaf thus behyght lorde prophete sayenge thus quacū que hora conuersus fuerit peccator ingemuerite xx viii vita viuit nō morietur tyme synful man tourned god fro synne haue sorow therfore shal lyue shal deye endelesly syde lyuyth dedely synne wyl leue ne amē de hym therof ne receyue sacrament penaunce elles yf receyue takyth sothfastly loue god loue vertue clennesse oonly drede shame worlde drede on̄ly paynes helle refourmed lyknesse ceyued fals crysten mā yt hath ben encōbred dedely syn al lyfe tyme refourmed ī soule withī vnperceyuably takē tournyng wyl thorough pryue myght gracyous werchyng ye holy ghost yt sodēly werchyth tyme monent twynkelynge eye ryghtyth frowarde soule tourneth fro ghostly fylth fayrnes vnseable seruaūt ye fende makyth son ioye ye prysoner helle makyth perceyuer heuēly herytage ayēstōdyng al ye flesshly felyng synful ymage yt ye bodely kynde thou shalt vnderstōde yt ye sacramēt baptym penaūce yt vertu lete destroy vtterly al ye styrynges flesshly lustes paynful passyons yt mānes soule neuer fele maner rysyng ne styrynges hē tyme yf soule fully refourmed ye worshyp ye fyrst makyng yt may fully ī lyf ye vertu yt clēseth soule fro al syn̄es done yf departed fro ye body sauyth fro dāpnacyon yf dwelle ye body yeuyth ye soule grace ayenstōde ye styrynges syn kepyth grace also yt maner lusty styrynges passyons yt felyth ye flesshe neuer greuous shal dere ne departe fro god aslōge wylfully senteth therto thus saynt poul meaned whā sayd thꝰ nichil dāpnacōnis htis q̄ nō scdm carnē ambulant isro viiii thyse soules yt arn refourmed ye ymage god feyth thorugh sacrament baptym penaūce shal dampned felynges ymage syn̄e yf yt go ye styryuges ye flesshe dede doyng ¶that sholde beleue stedfastly refourmynge ymage yf cōscience wytnes v ful forsakyng synne true tornyng wyl good lyuyng ca ix refourmynge fayth spekyth saynt poul thushebr̄ x iustus ex fide viuit ryghtwysman lyueth fayth made ryghtful baptym penaunce lyueth fayth whiche suffyseth vnto saluacyō heuenly pee saynt poul sayth iustificati ex fide pacē habemus ad deū isro v yt arn ryghted refourmed thorugh faythe cryst hathe pee accorde made betwyx god v nought ayenstondyng yt vycyous felynges body syn though refourmyng pryue maye wel felte lyf neuertheles trowyth stedfastly shapyth werkes bysely accorde trouth yt tourne ayen dedely syn̄e soothly whan y• houre deth comyth soule departed fro bodyly lyf shal fynde sooth yt saye thus sayd saynt iohn̄ cōforte chosen soules yt lyuen ī fayth vnder ye felyng paynful ymage karissimi nunc sumus filii dei sed non dū aparuit quod erimus scimus autē qm̄ cū cristus apparuit tunt apparebimus cum eo simile et gloria dere frendes arn whyle lyue ye sōnes god arn refourmed faythe cryst lyckenes shewyth yet arn al pryue neuertheles knowe wel yt whā lorde shal shewe hym laste daye shal appere hym lyke vnto hym endles ioye thou wolte wyte then̄e yf thy soule refourmed ymage god yt haue sayd thou maye haue entree ransake thy conscyence loke thy wyl stondeth al tourned fro al maner dedely synne thou woldest thynge wyttyngly wylfully breke y• therfore hym nedeth euer striuyng fightynge ayenst wycked styrynges ymage synne yt make none accorde therwith ne take noo frendshyp buxum vnskylful biddynges begyleth hymselfe soothly yf stryueth hem hym nedeth moche drede assentynge stryfe brekyth pee fals accorde good man haue pee al thynge sauf ye fende ymage synne ayenste hem hym nedeth euer fyght thoughte dede tyl haue geten hem maystry yt shall neuer fully lyfe longe hereth felyth ymage saye y• soule maye thornghe grace haue hyer honde ouer ymage ferforthe yt shall folowe ne sente vnskylful styrynges clene delyuerde fro ymage sholde fele suggestyon ne ianglyng flesshly affeccyon ne vayne thought tyme maye man haue lyfe hope yt soule refourmed felynge rauysshynge loue contemplacyon god may ferre fro sensualyte fro vayne ymagynacyon ferre drawen departe fro flesshly felynge tyme shall fele god lasteth euer therfore saye euery man behouyth stryffe ayenst ymage synne namely refourmed fayth oonly soo lyghtly maye dysceyued therwith ye person whiche mē sayth saynt poul caro concupiscit aduersꝰ spiritū spūs aduersꝰ carnē gal v soule refourmed ye lyknes god fyghtyth ayēst yt flesshly styrynges ymage synne also ymage synne stryueth ayenst wyll spyryte manere fyghtyng dowble ymage saynt poule knewe whā sayd thus inueni legem membris mei repugnantē legi mētis mee capitiuum meducentē legem peccati haue founde two lawes one lawe soule within another flesshly lym̄es without fyghtyng yt ofte ledeth wretchyd prysoner ye lawe syn thyse two lawes soule vnderstonde double ymage ro vii lawe spyryte vnderstonde y• reason soule whan refourmed ye ymage god lawe flesshe vnderstonde ye sensualytees whiche calle y• ymage synne thyse two lawes soule refourmed ledeth lyfe saynt poul sayth mēte enim seruio legi dei carne enim legi peccati soule wyl reason serue lawe god flessh yt ī flesshly appetyte serue lawe synne neuertheles yt soule refourmed shal dispeyre thoughe serue lawe synne felynge vycyous sensualyte ayenste wyl spyryte cause corrupcyon bodely kynde saynt poul excusyth sayeng thus owne persone ro vii non enī quod volo bonū hoc ago sed malum quod odi hoc facio si autē malū quod odi hoc facio nō ego operor illud sed quod habitat ī peccatū good yt wolde wolde fele flesshly styryng doo euyl yt hate synful styryng flesshe hate yet fele hem neuertheles syth yt haue ye wycked styrynges flesshe yet fele hem ofte delyte hem ayenst wyl shal reherced ayenste fro dampnacyon yf hadde done hem corrupcyon ymage synne doth hem loo saynt poul persone god yf deye yt plyght shall saaf trouth shal saue hym trouth dede lackyth loue therfore seruyth hym haue trouth quyckened loue charyte arn refourmed lyckenesse god though leest degre charyte arn symple soules ye whiche felen ye yeft specyal deuocyon ne ghostly knowyng god ghostly men done trowen generally holy chyrche trowyth knowyth fully yt nedeth hem trowyth kepe hem loue charytee euen crysten maye fleen al dedely synne cūnynge dooen ye dedes mercy euen crysten al thyse longen blysse heuen wrytten apocapoc iꝯ thus qui timetis deum pusilli et magni lau • ate eum ye dreden god bothe smale grete thanke hym grete arn vnderstode soules yt arne profytyng grace elles perfyte ye loue god whiche arn refourmyd ghostly felynge • male arn vnderstō de soules vnperfyte worldly men wymmen haue chyldys knowynge god ful lytyl felynge hym arn brought forth bosom holy chyrche nourysshed sacrament chylderne arn fedde mylke al thyse sholde loue god thanke hym saluacyon soules endles mercy goodnesse holy chyrche moder al thyse hath tender loue al chylderne ghostly prayeth asketh hem al tenderly spowse ihesu geteth hem hele soule thorough vertue passyon namly hem speke hemselfe ghostly prayer nede thus fynde gospel y• woman chanee asked lorde hele doughter traueyled fende lorde made fyrst daungeour cause alyene neuertheles ceased cry tyl lorde graūted askyng sayd thus aa woman moche thy trouth ye ryght thou wolt hour doughter hole woman betokenith holy chyrche y• asketh helpe lorde symple vncūnynge soules traueyled tēptacyon ye worlde speke perfytly god feruour deuocōn ne brennyng loue contēplacyon though seme lorde make daūgeour fyrste cause arn alyened fro hym neuerthelesse grete trouthe dyserte holy chyrche graunteth al yt wyll arn thyse symple soules yt trowen stedfastly holy chyrche trowyth putten hem fully ye mercy god maken hem vnder sacrament lawes holy chyrche made saaf thorugh prayer trouth moder holy chyrche ¶that soules refourmed neden euer fyght stryue ayenste styrynges synne whyle lyuen soule maye knowe whan assentyth ye styrynge whan caplm̄ xi refourmyng fayth lyghtly goten maye lyghtly beholde therfore mā woman yt refourmed lyekenesse god trouth moche traueyle besynesse must haue yf wyl kepe ymage hole clene yt falle downe ayen thorugh wekenesse wyl ymage syn̄e maye ydle ne reklees ye ymage synne nere festnyd hym contynually pressyth vpon hym dyuerse styrynges syn yf right wel waar shal ful lyghtly thorugh assent fal ayē ther comforteth al soules thorough grace arne refourmed fayth y• sholden tomoche drede ye bourden ymage vnskylful styrynges therof yf sente wylfully therto neuertheles poynte many soules y• arne refourmed trouthe arne oft tymes moche tormented trowbled vayne thus whan haue felte flesshly styrynges pryde enuye couetyse lechery ony desyn̄e wote somtyme whether sent therto grete wōder tyme temptacyon freel mannes thought trowbled ouer layed yt hath clere syght ne fredom hymself taken oft lykyng vnwarly gooth forth grete whyle perceyue therfore fallen dowte dwere wheder syn̄ed tyme tēptacyon ayenst poynt saye thynke yt soule maye haue assayeng manere whed yt assente yt man styred ony maner synne lykynge soo grete flesshly felynge yt trowblyth reason maystry ocupyeth affeccōn ye soule neuertheles kepyth hym yt foloweth dede ne wolde yf myght rather paynful hym fele lykyng ye synne fayne wolde put awaye yf myght whan ye styryng ouerpassed glad wel payed yt delyuered assay may wyte yt lykyng neuer grete flesshly felynge yt assented ne synned namly dedely neuertheles remedye syker suche symple soule yt marred helpe yt bolde hymself vtterly wenynge y• suche flesshly styryng lykyng syn̄eh myght falle rechelesnes fals sekernes ne also yt dredeful ne symple wytte deme hem al dedely synne grete venyals nother soth yt holde hē al syn̄es wretchydnes hymself haue sorowe hē besy deme hem nother dedely ne venyall yf conscience gretly greued y• hastely go shewe confessour general specyal suche styrynges namly euery styrynge ye begynneth festen ony rote ye herte moost ocupyeth drawe downe synne worldly vanytee whan thus shryuen generally specyally trow stedfastly y• ben foryeuen dyspute nomore hem arne passed foryeuen whether dedely venyal yt besy kepe hym better ayenst hem arne comyng yf thus maye come reste conscyence arn flesshly vncūnyng wolde fele see foryeuenes syn̄es opē ly myght fele see bodely thynge moche fele therfore falle ofte suche weeres doubtes hymself neuer maye come reste arne vnwyse faythe gooth felyng lorde sayd man ye palsye whan helyd hym thus cōfide sili remiremittū • tibi pccā tuam ix sone trowe stedfastly thy syn̄es arn foryeuen y• sayd hym se fele thy syn̄es arne foryeue y• ye foryeuenes syn̄es doon ghostly vnseable thorough grace ye holy ghost trowe ryght wyse euery man wyl come reste conscyence hym behouyth fyrst yf y• hym trowe without ghostly felynge foryeuenes synnes yf fyrste trowe shal afterwarde thorough grace fele vnderstonde soo thus sayth apostle nisi crederitis nō intellegitis isisay vii yf ye fyrst trowe ye maye vnderstonde trouth gooth vnderstondynge comyth whiche vnderstondynge calle lyght god yf gracyous soule maye haue thorough grete clennessem v oure lorde sayth beati mundo corde qm̄ ip̄i deum videbunt blessyd clene herte shall see god flesshly eye inner eye vnderstondyng clensed lyghted thorough grace holy ghost se sothfastnes ye whiche clennes soule maye fele yf haue stable trouth goynge thapostle sayth fide mundans corda eo rum act xv lorde clenseth ye hertes chosen thoroughe fayth therfore nedful yt soule trowe fyrst refourmynge hymself made thorough sacramente penaunce though see dyspose hymselfe fully lyue ryghtfully vertuously tronth askyth soo maye come syght refourmynge felynge ¶that ymage bothe fayre fowle whyles lyfe though refourmed dyuersyte felynges pryuely betwene thyse soules ben refourmed yt ben caplm̄ xii fayr mannes soule fowle mannes soule fayr moche refourmed fayth ye lyckenes god foule moche medlyd flesshly felynges vnskylful styrynges ofth ymage syn foule without beest fayr withī lyke āgel foule felyng sensualyte fayre trouth reason foule flesshly appetyte fayre good wyl thus fayre thus foule chosen soule sayenge holy wrytte thus nigra sū sed formosa filie ierlm sicut tabernacula cedar et sicut pellis salomonis iscant blacke fayre shaply ye doughter ihr̄lm ye tabernacle cedar skynne salomon ye angel heuen y• arne doughters hye ier̄lm wonder mene dyspyse blacke shadowe though blacke without cause flesshly kynde tabernacle cedar neuertheles ful fayre skynne salomon refourmed lyckenes god cedar vnderstōde reproued soule whiche tabernacle deuyll salomon vnderstōde lorde ihesu pee peasyble skynne salomon vnderstonde blessyd anget lorded wellyth hydde lyfe hydde skyn̄e quycke body therfore aungel lyckened skynne thenne maye chosen soule meke truste god gladenes herte saye thus though blacke cause body synne reproued soule one tabernacle fende neuertheles within ful fayre thoroughe trouthe good wyll lyke angel heuen sayth nother place nolite considerare qd fusca sūcant qm̄ decolorauit sol beholde swart y• sonne hath defaded sonne makyth askynne swarte oonly without within betokenith flesshly lyfe therfore sayth chosen soule thus repreue swart swartnesse y• haue al without towchynge berynge ymage synne thynge within therfore soothly though yt chosen soule refourmed fayth dwelle body synne fele flesshly styrynges vse y• bodely werkes doth tabernacle cedar ferforth y• mānes dome sholde dyfference bytwyx yt one neuertheles within soules full grete deuersyte syght god full moche twynnynge knowynge whiche one whiche oonly kepte god passeth mannes dome mannes felynge therfore shall man deme euyl thynge maye vsed bothe euyll well soule refourmed take fully loue worlde moche ouerlayed lykynge flesshe al sensualyte chesyth ful rest herte pryue meanynge wolde elles haue yt myght euer syker therof felyth lycour grace styryng hym lothe flesshly lyf ne desyre heuenly blysse therfore maye saye bereth ymage syn̄e borne man seke weyke myght bere hymselfe therfore layed bedde borne lytere ryght suche synful soule weyke vnmyghty lackynge grace maye neyther meue honde ne fote ouy good dede ne ayenstonde dysplesynge wyl leest styryng synne whan comyth falleth downe therto beest vpon careyne soule refourmed though vse flesshly wyttes fele flesshly styrynges neuertheles lotheth hem herte wolde thynge fully reste hem fleeth reste byttynge adder leuer haue reste y• loue herte god yf yt cowde somtyme desyreth therto often grutcheth lykynge lyfe loue lyfe euerlastyng soule borne ymage synne seke man thoughe fele beryth thorugh grace made myghty stronge suffre bere body al euyl styringes without hurtynge defoylynge hymself y• asmoche loueth hem ne foloweth hē ne senteth hem whiche arne dedely synnes nother dooth bodely fulfylled y• gospell man y• palsye feble y• myght go therfore layed borne lytere brought lorde whan lorde sawe hym myscheyf goodnesse sayd hym surge et tolle grabatum tuū et vade domum cuā isioh ryse vp take thy bedde go thy hous dyde hole sothly ryght man bare vpon backe whan made hole bedde bare hym ryght maye sayd ghostly soule refourmed faythe beryth ymage synne whiche bare hym therfore adradde moche thy blackenesse thou haste berynge ymage synne ayenste ye shame dyscomforte thou haste beholdyng also ayen vpbraydynge thou felyst thy hert ghostly enmyes whan sayd thus thy lorde ihesus sekest thou ye fayrnes y• thou spekest felyst thou ought blyndnes synne ymage god thou sayest refourmed comforte thyselfe faythful styfly haue sayd yf thou thou shalt trouth destroye al temptacyons thin enmyes thus sayd apostle poul accipe scutum fidei quo omnia tela hostis nequissima poteris extinguere iseph ꝯ take ashelde stedfaste trouth thorugh whiche thou maye quenche al brennynge dartes thyn enmye ¶ thre manere men ye whiche ben refourmed ben refourmed on̄ly fayth fayth felynge caplm̄ xiii bi haue sayd maye thou see dyuers partyes soule arn dyuers state men men arn refourmed lykenesse god arne refourmed lyckenesse god arn refourmed on̄ly fayth arne refourmed fayth felynge thou shalt vnder stonde yt soule hath two partyes one called sensualyte flesshly felynge fyue outwarde wyttes whiche comon man beest whiche sensualyte whan vnskylfully vnordynatly ruled made ymage synne whan ruled reason thenne sensualyte syn̄e partye called reason departed two ouer partye y• nether ouer party lyckened man sholde mayster souereyne propyrly ymage god on̄ly soule knowyth god louyth hym neyther lyckened woman sholde burum ouer partye reyson woman buxum man lyeth knowynge rulynge erthly thynges vse hem dyscretly nede refuse hē whan nede haue euer eye vpwarde ouer partye reasō drede reuerence folow may say y• soule lyueth lykynges lustes flesshe vnskylful beest neyther hath knowynge god ne desyre vertues ne good lyuynge al blynded pryde frette enuy ouerlayed whth couetyse defoyled lecherye grete synnes refourmed ye lyckenesse god lyeth resteth fully ymage synne sensualyte nother soule dredeth god ayenstondeth dedely styrynges sensualyte foloweth hem lyueth resonably ruelynge gouernaūce worldly thynges setteth entent wyl pleyse god outwarde werkes refourmed lyknesse god faythe though fele styrynges synne ye dooth shal dysease hym heresteth hem dooth nother soule fleeth thorugh grace al dedely styrynges sē sualyte venyals also ferforth yt felyth hem refourmed felynge folowyth ye ouerparty reason beholdyng god ghostly thynges shal tel afterwarde ¶how men ben synne forshapen hemselfe dyuerse bestes lyckenesse bē called louers worlde caplm̄ xiiii wretchyd man knowyth y• worthynesse soule ne wyll knowe moost worthy creature euer god made take angel lyke to▪ hye aboue al kynde bodely whiche thynge maye suffyse full reste oonly god therfore sholde nothynge loue ne lyke hym oonly ne coueyte ne seke myght refourmed lyknes knowyth therfore sekyth coueytyth rest lykynge outwarde bodely creature werse hym self unkyndly doth vnresouably werkyth y• leuyth ye souereyn good euerstyng lyfe yt god vnsought vnloued vnknowen vnworshypped chesyth reste blysse passynge delyte erthely thyng neuerthelesse thus done al ye louers worlde haue ioye blysse wretchyd lyfe haue pryde vaynglory hemself ye whan haue loste drede god traueyle studye nyght day mow come worshyp praysynge worlde maken noo force soo myght come therto ouerpasse al men eyther clergy crafte name fame ryches reuerence souerente maystershyp hye state lordshyp mē haue reste ryches outragious hauour erthly good setten hertes fully gete y• seke elles myght come therto haue lykynge flesshly lustes glotenye lecherye bodely vnclennes oo thynge nother thus wretchydly thyse y• done thus forshapen hemself fro worthynes mā torne hem dyuers bestes lyckenes prowde man torned lyon pryde wolde drade worshypped men man ayenstonde ye fulfyllynge flesshly wyl nother worde ne dede yf ony man wolde lette mysproude wyl weryth felle wrothe woll wroken hym lyon wrekith hym lytyl beest mā dooth thus man dooth vnresonably ayenst y• kynde man tourned transfourmed lyon enuyous angry men arne torned hoūdes thoroughe wrathe enuye ye brekyth ayen euen cristē bytyth hē wycked malycyous wordes greuyth hem yt haue trespassed wrongfull dedes harmyng hem body soule ayenst goddis byddynge men arne forshapen ass ye arne slowe ye seruyce god euyl wylled ony good dede euen crysten arne redy ynough ren̄e worldly profyte erthly worshyp pleysaū ce erthly man ghostly mede helpe owne soules ye worshyp god soone yrke wol therof yf ought done goon pase frowarde wyl torned swyne blynde wytte bestly maners haue drede god folowen on̄ ly lustes lykynges flesshe haue rewarde honeste man ne rule hem byddynge reason ne restrayne vnskylfull styrynges flesshly kynde assone flesshly styrynge comyth synne redy falle ther folowe swyne done men torned wulfes lyuen raueyn fals couetous men done thorough maystry ouerledyng robben euē crysten worldly goodes men torned fox fals men deceyuable men lyuen trecherye gyle al thyse many moo yt lyuen drede god breken cōmaūdementes forshapen hemself fro lyknes god maken hem lyke bestes ye worse bestes lyke fende helle therfore sothly thyse men yt lyuen thus yf ben refourmed whan hour deth cometh soules hem departed fro ye bodyes shal eye opened yt nowe stopped synne thenne shal fele fynde payne wretchydnes lyued asmoche ye ymage god refourmed thorugh sacrament penaunce hem neyther fayth ne felynge lyfe shal cursed caste fro ye blessyd face creatour shal dampned y• deuyl depnes helle without ende thus sayth saynt iohn̄ thapocalipse tumidis et incredulis execratis homicidis fornicatoribus venificis ydolatris om̄ibꝭ mendacibꝭ par illorum erit stagno ardenti igne sulphureapoc ir prowde men mystrowyng men cursed men sleers lecherous couetous poyseners worshyppers mawmentes al fals lyers dele shal ye deuyl pytte helle brennyng fyre brymston ye louers worlde wolde oft thynke al worlde shal passe drawe ende al wycked loue shal harde punysshed sholde within shorte tyme loth al worldly lustes yt lyke sholde lyfte vp herte loue god wolde besyly seke traueyle myght refourmed lyckenes passe hen ¶how louers worlde vnable hem dyuers maners refourmynge owne soule capitulum xv sayth hem thus wolde fayne loue god good man forsake ye loue worlde yf myght haue grace therto grace good man hath sholde dooth haue therfore maye wyte excused vnto thyse mē say • hꝰ • h saye yt haue grace therfore lyen styl synne maye ryse auayleth hem ayenst god owne defawte vnable hem dyuers wayes moche lyght grace maye shyne hem nerest hertes fro warde yt wol grace haue ne wol gode men wote well yf sholde good men must nedes forbere grete lykynge luste worlde haue erthly thynges yt wol hē thken swete yt wol forgo also must nedes take werkes penaūce fastyng wakyng prayeng many good dedes doyng chastisynge theyr flessh ī withdrawyng theyr flesshly wyll yt maye made sharpe dredful thynkyng vggen lothen thynke vpon cowardly wretchydly dwel stelle synne wolde haue grace semyth begynnen able hem therto wyll wonder weeke assone ony styrynge synne comyth though contrary byddyng god falle anone therto bounde thorugh custome oft fallynge ofte assentynge synne ye hem thynke impossyble ayenstonde soo feyned herdnes perfourmynge weekyth wyl smytyth downe ayē also felen styryng grace whan haue bytyng conscyēce euyl lyuynge sholde leue paynful hē heuy wol suffre ne abyde fle therfro foryete yf may ferforth seke lykynge comforte outwarde flysshly creature sholde fele bytynge conscyence within soule ouer men blynde bestly wene none lyfe ne yt soule beest yt ye soule man deyeth ye body ye soule beest therfore saye ete drynke make mery lyfe ben syker see none heuen sothly suche wretch sayen thus hertes though saye mouth whiche men prophete sayth thus dixit incipiēs corde suo nō est deus ye vnwyse man sayd hertep noo god vnwyse man euery wretchyd man lyueth loueth syn̄e chesyth ye loue worlde rest soule sayth god mouth wol speke hym sō tyme whan fareth wel flesshly reuerence whan sayth blessyd god somtyme dyspyte whan angry ayenst god euen crysten sweryth blessyd body ony mēbres sayth ī thought yt god eyther weneth yt god seeth synne wyll punysshe harde holy wrytte sayth wol foryeue hym ye synne though see elles y• shal crysten man dāpned neuer euyl elles yf fast lady fast saye euery daye certeyn oryson euery day ii mass iii▪ certeyn bodely dede worshyp god shall neuer go helle neuer somoche synne though forsake man sayth herte god vnwyse ye prophete sayth shall fele fynde payne yt god forgate set nought sette wele worlde prophete sayth sola vexacio dabit intellectū auditu • isi xx viii oonly payne shal yeue vnderstondynge knowyth ne wol knowe shal wel knowe whan payne ¶a lytyl coūseyle howe louers worlde sholde yf wol refourmed soule byfore partynge hen caplm̄ xvi thyse men though wote wel arne grace dedely synne haue care ne sorowe ne thought therfore make flesshly myrth worldly solace asmoche maye ferder ben fro grace ye myrth make perchaūce holden hem wel payd yt haue grace yt maye fully freely folow ye lykynge flesshly lustes though god slepe myght see hem one moost defawte yt maye thus owne frowardnes stop lyght grace fro owne soule yt maye reste therin whiche grace asmoche shyneth al ghostly creature redy entre receyued ye sonne shyneth ouer al creature bodely letted thꝰ sayth saynt iohn̄ ī ye ghospeliohīsi lux tenebris lucet • enebre eā non cōprehenderūt lyght grace shyneth derkenes mē ne hertes derke thorugh synne derknesse taketh thyse blynde hertes receyue ye gracyous lyght ne haue profyte ryght blynde man vmbi • apped lyght ye sonne whan stōdeth therin yet seeth ne hath profyte ther go therby ryght soo ghostly soule blynded dedely syn̄e al vmbylapped ghostly lyght yet neuer better blynded wol see ne knowe blyndenesse yt one moost lettynge grace wretchyd man wol knowe owne blyndnesse pride hymself elles yf knowe chargeth makyth myrth game ouer al syker therfore vnto al thyse men thus blynded boūde loue worlde fowle forshape fro ye fayrhede man saye counseyle thynke soule yt able hem vnto grace asmoche may may vpon wyse yf wol whan fele hemself grace ouerlayed dedely synne thynke myscheyf peryl hem put grace departed fro god ben thynge holdeth hem fro pytte helle ne sholde ryght soone falle therin bare syngyl • hrede bodely lyfe wherby hange lyghtlyer may lost syngyl threde maye broken two breth stopped body maye lyghtly falle soule shal passe forth anone helle withoute ende yf wolde thynke thus sholde quake shake drede ryghtful dome god herde punysshynge synne sholde make sorow morne synne lackynge grace sholde crye pray yt myght haue grace yf dede thus thenne sholde grace falle put de • knesse hardnes herte weyknes wyl yeue hem myght strengthe forsake fals loue worlde moche dedely synne soule soo ferre fro god thorugh wyckydnesse wyl dedely synne take none lyueth body syn̄e ne may thorugh grace ryghted refourmed clennesse oflyuynge yf woll bowe wyl god mekenesse amende lyfe hertly axe grace foryeuenes hym excuse lorde fully accuse hymself holy wryt sayth nolo mortē pccōrissed magi vt cōuertat et viuat lorde sayth wol ye dethe synner wol yt torned lyue lorde wol moost frowarde man yt lyueth forshapen thorugh synne yf torne wyl aske grace refourmed lyknesse ¶that refourmyng fayth felyng may sodē ly goten grace moche bodely ghostly traueyle ī lengthe tyme caplm xvii refourmyng fayth haue sayd yt lyghtly may comyth refourmyng fayth felynge maye lyghtly begote thorugh longe trauyle moche besynesse refourmynge fayth comyn al chosen soules though ben lowest degree charyte refourmynge felynge specyally thyse soules yt may come state perfeccyon maye sodeynly grete plente grace moche ghostly traueyle soule maye come therto whan fyrste helyd ghostly syknes whan al bytter passyons flesshly lustes olde felynges arne brente oute herte fyre desyre newe gracyous felynges arne brought inne brennynge loue ghostly lyght then̄e ryght nyghe hygheth soule perfeccyon refourmynge felynge ¶for soth ryght man broughte nye deth thorough bodely syknesse though receyue medicyne whiche restored syker lyfe maye therfore anone ryse vp go werke hole maye feblenes body holdeth hym downe muste abyde good whyle kepe hym wel medicynes dyete hym mesure ye techynge leche tyl maye fully recouer bodely hele ryght ghostly brought ghostly dethe thorugh dedely synne though thorugh medycyne sacrament penaūce restored lyfe shal dampned neuertheles anone hole passyons al flesshly desyres ne able contemplacyon hym behouyth abyde grete whyle take good kepe hymselfe rule hym soo myght recouer ful hele soule shal langern grete whyle fully hole neuertheles yf take medecynes good leche vse hem tyme mesure dyscrecyon shall moche sooner restored ghostly strength come refourminge felynge refourmynge fayth ye lowest state al chosen soules byneth yt myght well refourmynge felyng hyest state lyfe soule maye come fro lowest ye hyest maye soule sodenly styrte mā wol clymbe vpon ladder hye setteth fote vpon lowest stele may nexte flee vp ye hyest hym behoueth go processe one nother tyl maye come ouerest ryght ghostly noo man made sodenly souereyne grace thorough longe exercyse slye werkynge soule maye come therto namly whan helpyth techyth wretchid soule whome al grace lyeth without specyal helpe inwardly techynge hym maye noo soule come therto ¶the cause fewe soules rewarde yt multytude comen refourmg fayth felynge caplm̄ xviii sayst thou syth lorde curteys goodnes gracyous yeftes free wonder fewe sowles semyth rewarde multytude maye come refourmynge felynge semyth yt dangerous sothe toke rewarde creature whiche takyng fayth become seruauntes unto may answere saye thynketh one enchesen many refourmed fayth setten hertes profyte grace ne seke none hyer estate good lyuynge thorugh besye traueyle prayeng thynkyng bodely ghostly werkynge hem thynke ynough hem kepe hemselfe dedely synne stonde stylle plyght saye ynough hem saaf haue leest degre heuen wol coueyte thus perchaunce dooth chosen soules leden worlde actyflyfe lytyl wonder hem occupyed worldly besynesse nedeth done maye fully sette hertes profyte ghostly tkynge neuertheles peryllous hem falle al daye nowe vp downe maye come stablenes gode lyuyng neuertheles somwhat excusable astate lyuynge men wymmen yt free fro worldly besynesse yf woll maye haue nedeful sustynaunce without grete bodely besynes specyally relygyous men wymmen may bynden hemselfe state perfeccyon takynge relygion men also seculer state haue moche reason grete kyndly wytte myght yf wolde dyspose hem come moche grace thyse men blame stōde stylle ydle wol prouffyte grace ne ferder sekynge come loue knowyng god sothly peryllous soule refourmed oonly sayth wol seke profyte ne yeue hym besyly ghostly traueyle maye lyghtly lese hath falle ayen dedely synne soule may stonde styl alwaye one state whyle flesshe eyther profytynge grace peyrynge syn̄e fareth hym dooth man drawe pytte whan vp wolde ferder go ye pyttes brynke sothly moche foole lytyl puffe wynde vnwarly styryng hȳ selfe sholde soone caste hym downe ayen wors byfore neuertheles yf fle fro ye brynke ferre maye go forth erthe though come grete storme syker falleth pytte ryght ghostly drawen ye pytte synne thoroughe refourmynge faythe whan dedely synne thynketh hymselfe syke • ynoughe therfore wol profyte holde hym stylle pyttys brynke nere maye sothely wyse atte leest temptacyon hys enmye hys flesshe falleth synne ayen neuerthelesse yf flee fro pytte yf sete herte fully com̄ grace traueyle besyly howe maye come therto yeue hym hertly prayeng thynkyng good werkes doyng though grete tēptacōns ryse ayenste hym fallyth lyghtly dedely synne ayen sothly wōder yt sythē grace good profytable mā whā hath lytyl therof ye lytyl yt myȝt lesse haue yt wol say ho wol haue ynough whan se worldly mā though haue worldly good moche hym nedeth yet wol neuer saye hoo haue ynough wol wol coueyte traueyle wyttes myghtes neuer woll stynte coueytyse tyl maye haue moche thenne sholde chosen soule coueyte ghostely good yt euerlastyng makyth soule blessyd neuer sholde cease coueytyng yf dyde wel▪ gete gete myght ye coueyteth shal haue sothly yf dyde thꝰ sholde profyte wexe grace gretly ¶a nother cause also ye wylful bodely customes indyscretly rewarded vsed somtyme hyndren soules fro felyng grace caplm̄ xix another enchesen mē refourmed fayth begynnynge tornyng god setten hemself certayn maner doyng whether bodely ghostly thynken euer kepe maner worchyng forth chaunge none ye comith thorugh grace though better wene yt doynge sholde beste hē alwaye holde therfore resten hem therin thorough custome bynde hem therto whan haue fulfylled thynke hem wonderly eased wene haue done grete thyng god perchaunce yf falle letted fro ye custome though skilful cause ben heuy angry haue troublynge conscyence▪ yf done grete dedely synne thyse men hyndren hemself somwhat fro felyng grace sette perfeccyon bodely werke make ende myddes waye none ende bodely customes men vse begynnyng good meanes wayes ledynge soule perfeccyon therfore sayth perfeccyon ī bodely werke ghostly werke felych ye begynnynge tornynge god woll fe • der seke euer rest therin hyndreth hymselfe gretly symple crafte prentyse euer lyke wyse fyrste daye moche thyrty wynter elles yf craft good subtyl dulle wytte elles euyl wyl profyteth therin thenne soth yt al craftes seruyse god moost souereyne moost subtyl hyghest hardest come perfeccyon also moost profytable moost wynnyng hym maye soth fastly performe therfore semyth prentises euer ylyke ferforth lernynge eyther dulle wytted elles euyll wylled repreue thyse customes men vse state begynnynge whether ben bodely ghostly say ful good spedfull hem vse wolde helde hem waye entre towarde ghostly felynge vsed hem couenable meane tyl better come vsynge hem coueyted better then̄e yf better come ghostly drawynge thought frō flesshlynes fro sensualyte vayn ymagynacion yf sholde letted cause customes yt leue custome whan maye lefte without scaunder dysease folowe fele yf neyther lette vse bothe yf maye meane customes nedeful thorugh bonde lawe rule penaunce wylfully taken thus techeth v prophete sawter sayeng thꝰ etem̄ benediccionem dabit legislator ibunt de virtute virtutem videbitur deus deo rum syon isp̄ lxxx iii sothly brynger lawe shal yeue blessyng shal go fro vertue vertue god goddys shal see syon brynger lawe lorde ihesu cryst shal yeue blessynge shal yeue hys grace chosen soules callynge hem fro synne ryghtynge hem good werkes lyckenesse thorugh whiche grace shall proufyte wexe fro vertue vertue tyll come syon tyl come contemplacyon whiche shal see god goddys shal see wel one god ¶how without moche bodely ghostly besynes without moche grace mekenesse soules may refourmed felynge ne kepe therin come therto caplm̄ xx sayest thou syth refourmyng faythe lowe peryllous rest cause drede fallynge agayne refourmynge felynge hyghe syker myght come therto thenne coueytest thou wyte manere traueyle moost spedful vse whiche man myghte prouffyte come therto yf ony certayne traueyle specyal dede whiche man myght come grace refourmynge felynge vnto saye thus thou wotest wel man woman wol dyspose hym come clennesse herte felynge grace hym behoueth haue moche traueylle grete fyghtynge wyl werke lastyngly agaynste wycked styrynges al hede synnes oonly ayenste pryde enuye ayenst al al spyces comen oute theym haue sayde fyrste wrytyng passyons flesshly desyres lette clennesse herte pee conscyence hym behoueth also traueyle gete al vertues oonly chastyte abstynence also pacyence myldenesse charite mekenesse al maye doon one maner werke dyuerse werkes many sundry dysposycyons men nowe prayenge nowe thynkynge worchynge good werkes nowe assayenge theym selfe dyuers wyse hunger thruste colde sufferyng shame dyspyte yf nede bodely dysease loue vertue sothfastnesse knowest thou wel redest thou euery boke techeth good lyuynge thus sayth euery mā wol styre mennes soules loue god semyth specyal traueyle ne certeyn dede thorugh whiche oonly soule myght come yt grace pryncypally thorugh grace lorde ihesu many dedes grete al yt may done yet al lytyl ynough one skylle may sith lorde ihū hymself specyal mayster crafte specyal leche ghostly lyknes without hym al nought therfore resonable techeth styreth man folowe werke symple mayster teche dyscyple whyle ī lernynge euer one lesson vnwyse leche one medecyne wol hele al sore therfore lorde ihesu wyse good shewe wysdom goodnes techeth dyuers lesson dissyples yt profyte lernynge yeueth dyuers soules sere dyuers medycynes felynge syknes also nother skylle ony certayne dede whiche soule myghte come perfyte loue god sholde man wene myght come therto owne werke thorugh owne traueyle marchaunt comyth mede owne traueyle oonly owne werke nay ghostly loue god wol serue god wysely come perfyte loue god shal coueyte haue none mede hym oonly haue hym may creature deserue oonly owne traueyle though man myght traueyle moche bodely ghostly al creature euer myghte myght deserue oonly werkes haue god mede souereyn blysse endles goodnes passyth without cōparyson al mēnes desertes therfore may gotē mannes specyal werkes bodely mede may free yeuyth hymsefe whet̄he wol whan wol neyther ne yt ne tyme ne yt tyme though soule worche ye may al hys lyfe tyme perfyte loue ihesu shall neuer haue tylle oure lorde ihesu woll freely yeue neuertheles syde saye also hope yeuyth yf man worche traueyle al maye ye tyll hym thynke maye elles ful wyl therto yf myght semyth yt neyther grace oonly without ful worchynge soule ne worchynge alone without grace bryngeth soule refourmynge felynge yt whiche refourmyng stondeth perfyte loue charite one ioyned grace ioyned worchynge bryngeth soule blessyd felynge perfyte loue whiche grace may restfully meke soules yt ben ful yt drede god therfore maye saye yt hath mekenes ne dooth besynes may come refourmyng felyng hath ful mekenes yt fele hymselfe soth fastly thus dooth al good dedes fastyng wakyng weryng heyre al suffryng bodely penaunce dooth al ye outwarde werkes mercy euen rrysten elles inwarde prayenge wepyng syghyng thynkyng yf rest euer hem leue somoche hem rewardeth hem gretly owne syght yt presumyth owne desertes thynketh hymselfe euer ryche good holy vertuous sothly aslonge felyth thus meke ynough ne though say thynke yt al dooth goddis yeft hymself yet meke ynough maye yet make hymself yet naked al good dedes ne make hym poore sothfastly spyrite ne fele hymselfe nought sothly vntyll soule fele ably thorugh grace nought hymself baren hym fro good dedes dooth thorugh beholdynge sothefastnes ihesu perfytly meke mekenes sothfastnes sothly nought elles therfore thorugh grace maye see ihesu howe dooth hymselfe dooth ryghte noughte suffreth ihesu worche hym hym lykyth meke ful harde impossyble vnresonable man wortheth al mannes reason seeth ferder doo many good dedes thenne ar rette alle ihesu sette hymselfe noughte neuertheles soo myght haue ghostly syghte soch fastnes hym sholde thynke ful true full resonable doo soo sothly hath syghte shal neuer lesse shal styred traueyle bodely ghostly moche ye ye better wyl may one cause men perauenture swinke swete pyne wretchyd body outragyous penaunce lyfe tyme euer sayeng orison sawters many bede yet maye come ghostly felyng loue god semyth done shorte tyme lesse payne haue mekenesse spake also tha syde saye dooth besynesse thynketh thus wherto sholde traueyle wherto sholde praye thynke wake faste ony bodely penaunce come suche grace sythen may goten ne oonly ye free yefte ihū therfore woll abyde flesshlynes ryght nought suche werkes bodely ne ghostly vntyl yeue yf woll yeue asketh noo worchynge lytyl y• shal haue yf wol yeue traueyle neuer fast therfore gete neuer sooner y• sayth thꝰ may come refourmyng drawyth hymself wylfully ydlenes flessheed vnableth hym yefte grace asmoche putteth fro hym inwarde werkynge stondyth lastynge desyre longynge ihesu outwarde werkyng traueyle body outwarde dedes soo maye haue therfore saye hath true mekenes ne ful hertly besynes inwarde on̄ly grete feruour lastynge desyre besye prayer thought god elles bothe inwarde outwarde may come ghostly refourmyng ymage ¶an entree howe soule shal haue menynge worchynge woll come refourmynge ensample apylgryme goynge iherusalem two maner mekenes caplm̄ xxi neuertheles thou coueytest haue maner worchynge whiche thou myght ye rather nyghen refourmynge shall saye thynketh grace lorde ihesu shortest y• redyest helpe knowe werchyng shal shal telle ensample good pylgryme vpon wyse man wolde go ierusalē knewe waye came nother man yt hoped knewe waye better thyder asked whyder myght come cyte man sayd hym myght come thyder without grete dysease moche traueyle waye longe peryllous full grete theues robber many lettynges ben fallen man goynge also manysere wayes semyth • edynge thyderwarde mē daye slayne dyspoyled maye come place coueyten neuerthelesse one waye whiche taketh holdeth wol vndertake sholde come cyte ierusalem sholde neūer lese lyf ne slayne ne deye defawte sholde ofte robbed euyl bete suffre moche dysese gooynge lyfe sholde saaf thenne sayd pylgryme maye haue lyfe saaf come place coueyte charge myschyef suffre goynge therfore say thou wolt sothly behote man answereth sayth thus lo sette yt ye ryght waye waye thou kepe lernynge teche y• thou herest seest felyst sholde lette waye abyde wylfully tary wylfully beholde lyke drede euer go forth thy waye thynke thou woldest iherusalem thou couetest thou desyrest nought elles yf men robbe dyspoyl bete scorne pyspyse ye stryue ayen yf thou wolte haue thy lyfe holde yt harme yt thou hast go forth nought yt thou take harme also yf men wol tary y• tale fede y• lesynges drawe yt myrthes leue thy pylgrymage make deefere answere ayen saye nought elles thou woldest ierusalem yf men profer ye yeftes wol make ryche worldly good rente hē thinke euer iherusalem yf thou wol holde way haue sayd vndertake thy lyfe yt thou shalt slayne thou shalt come ye place yt thou coueytest ghostly purpose ierusalem asmoche saye syght pea betokeneth contemplacyon perfyte loue god contemplacyon nought elles syght god whiche pee yf thou coueyte come blessyd syght pee true pylgryme ihr̄lm warde though yt neuer neuertheles ferforth shal set yt ye waye thyderwarde begynnyng ye hyghe waye ye whiche thou shalt go refourmyng fayth groūded mekely ye fayth ye lawes holy chyrche haue sayd trust sykerly though thou haue syn̄ed yf thou refourmed sacrament penaūce ye lawe holy chyrche yt thou art ye ryght way thē sythē thou arte ye syker way yf thou wol speke thy goyng make good iournayes ye behoueth holde thise ii thynges oftē thy mynde meknes loue yt nought haue nouȝt coueyte nought one thou shalt haue ye meanyng thyse wordes ī thyn entent habyt thy soule lastyngly though thou haue hem euer specyally thy thought yt nedeth mekenes sayth nought haue nouȝt loue sayth coueyte nought one yt ihū thyse two strē ge wel festned ye mynde ihesu makyth good corde ye harpe soule whan ben craftly towched ye fynger reason ye lower thou smytes vpō ye one ye hyer sowneth ye lesse thou felyst yt thou art yt thou hast thyself thorugh mekenes ye thou coueytest haue ihū desyre loue mene on̄ly ye mekenes yt soule felyth ye syght owne syn̄e freelnes wretchydnes lyfe ye wretchydnes euen crystē though mekenes sothfast medycynable neuertheles boystous flesshly regarde clene ne softe ne louely meane also mekenes yt soule felyth thorugh grace syght beholdyng ye endles beynge thyn owne herte fareth werkes desyre dooth styckes fyre styckes layed ye fyre gretter fyre ryght ye dyuers ghostly workynge yt man hathe thought kepe hole desyre ye myghtyer brennyng shal desyre god therfore loke wysely werke thou canst beste ye moost helpyth saue hole desyre ihū yf thou free art boū de vnder ye comyn lawe yt bynde yt wylfull customes vnchaūgably sholde lette ye fredom thyn herte loue ihū yf grace wolde vysyte yt specyally shal tel whiche customes euer gode nedeful kept loo suche custome euer good holde ye stondeth getyng vertue lettyng syn̄e ye custome sholde neuer lelft thou shal euer meke pacyent sobre chast yf thou wel al vertues custome nother thynge yt lettyth better gode leue whan tyme man may thus man haue custome saye thꝰ many beedes thynke maner thought thus long time wake knele thus long ony suche bodely dede custome leue somtyme whan resonable cause lettith elles yf grace comith otherwyse ¶of taryenges tēptacyons ye soules fele ghostly enmyes ghostly knowyng goyng ihrlm remedyes ayenst hem caplm̄ xxii art thou ye way woost thou shalt go beware enmyes yt wol besy lette yt yf maye entente putte thyn herte desyre ye longynge thou hast loue ihū dryue home ayen ye loue worldly vanyte thyng greueth hem moche thyse enmyes pryncypally flesshly desyres vayne dredes yt rysen thyn herte thorugh corrupcyon thy flesshly kynde wolde lette thy desyre loue god myght fully restfully occupye thyn herte thyse thy next enmyes also enmyes vnclene spyrytes besy sleyghtes wyles dysceyue one remedye shalt thou haue sayd yt saye trowe hem holde forth thy waye on̄ly desyre ye loue ihū answere euer thus nought haue nought coueyte nought oonly loue lorde ihū thyn enmyes saye fyrste thus styrynges herte yt thou art shryuen aryght olde synne hyd thyn hert yt thou knowest ne neuer shryuen aryght therfore thou must torne home ayen leue thy desyre goo shryue ye better trowe sayeng fals thou art shriuē trust sykerly yt thou art ye waye yt nedeth ransakynge shryfte yt passyd holde forth thy way thynke ihr̄lm also yf saye thou art worthy haue ye loue god wherto shalt thou couete thou mayst haue ne art worthy therto trowe hem go forth saye thus worthy vnworthy therfore wolde loue god yf yt sholde make worthy sythen made therto though sholde neuer haue yet wol coueyte therfore wol praye thynke myght gete yf thyn enmyes see yt thou begynnest wexe bolde wel wylled thy werke begyn wexe aferde neuertheles wol cease taryenge whan maye longe thou art goynge waye drede manassynge one syde flaterynge fals pleysyng yt syde make ye breke thy purpose torne home ayen wol saye thus thou holde forth thy desyre ihesu fully trauelyng thou begynnest thou shalt falle sykenes fantasyes frenesyes thou seest yt don̄ thou shalt fal pouertee bodely myscheyf man shal wel helpe thou myght falle priue temptacyons fende thou shalt helpe thyself wonder peryllous ony man yeue hym fully loue god leue worlde thynge coueyte oonly loue hym many perylles maye falle yt man knoweth therfore torne home ayen leue desyre thou shal neuer brynge ende worldly men done thus sayen thyn enmyes trowe hē holde thy desyre saye elles thou woldest haue ihesu ihr̄lm yf perceyue thy wyl stronge y• thou wolt spare synne ne syknes fantasyes ne frenesyes dowtes ne dredes ghostly tēptacyons myscheyf ne pouerte lyfe ne deth euer forth thou wolt one thynge thynge one make deefere hem though thou herde hem holdest forthe styfly thy prayer thyn ghostly werkes without styntynge dyscrecyon coūseyle thy souereyne thy ghostly fader begyn wrothe go lytyl nerer begyn robbe bete al shame whan make al dedes yt thou doost ben neuer wel done deuyed men euyl torned wors partye euer yt thou woldest haue done helpe thy body thy soule shal letted hyndred men yt thou shalt put fro thy wyl ī al thyng yt thou skyfully coueytes al don̄ yt thou sholdest styred yre malēcoly euyl wyl ayenst thyn euen crysten ayēst al thyse dyseases al thou may fele vse remedye take ihū thy mynde anger hem tarye hem thynke thy lessō yt thou art nought yt thou hast nought thou may nouȝt lese erthly good thou coueytest nought ye loue ihū holde forth thy waye ihr̄lm thy occupacyon neuertheles yf thou taryed somtyme thorugh freelte thyself suche vneases fallen thy bodely lyfe thorugh euyl wyl man malyce fende assone thou may come ayen thyself leue thy thynkyng thy dysease go forth thy werke abyde longe hem drede thyn enmyes ¶of general remedy ayēst wycked styrynges paynful taryenges yt fallē hertes ye flesshe ye worlde fende caplm xxiii whan thin enmyes see thou arte wel wylled thou arte angry heuy ne wrothe ne moche styred ayenste noo creature oughte maye doo speke ayenste • settest thy herte fully suffre maye falle ease vnease praysynge lackynge thou wolt charge noo thynge thou myghte kepe thy thoughte thy desyre hoole loue god thenne moche abasshed thenne woll assaye flaterynge vayne pleysynge whan brynge syghte thy soule al thy good dedes vertues bere vpon men praysen speke good thy holynes howe men loue worshyppe thy holy lyuynge thus done thyn enmyes thou sholdest thynke sayenge soth haue delyte vayne ioye reste therin yf thou wel thou shalt holde al suche iangelynge falsed flaterynge thyn enmye profereth drynke venym tempered honye therfore refuse saye thou wol therof thou wolde iherusalem suche lettynge thou shalt fele elles lyke thy flesshe worlde fende moo maye reherce man longe suffreth thought wylfully renne aboute worlde beholdynge sondry thynges perceyueth fewe lettynges assone drawyth al thought yernynge one thynge oonly haue yt knowe loue oonly ihesu shal wel fele many paynful lettynges euery thynge felyth yt coueyteth lettynge hym therfore haue tolde specyally example ouermore saye generally styrynge thou felyst thy flesshe fende pleysaunte paynful bytter swete lykynge dredful gladsom sorowful wolde drawe downe thy thought thy desyre fro loue ihesu worldly vanyte lette vtterly thy ghostly couetyse thou haste loue hym thy herte sholde occupyed styrynge restyngly sette nought receyue wylfully tarye therwith longe yf worldly thyng ye behoueth nedes done thy selfe thyn euen crysten spede soone brynge ende yt hange thyn herte nother thynge yt nedeth elles wcheth charge iangyll therwith ne angre drede lyke smyte thyn herte redely saye thus nought haue nought nought seke ne coueyte loue ihesu knyght thy thought desyre strength maynten prayer ghostly werkes thou forgete shal lede thy ryght waye saue fro al perylles though thou fele hem thou shalt perisshe hope shal brynge perfyte loue lorde ihū neuertheles syde saye also werke styrynge maye helpe thy desyre strengthe nourysshe make thy thought ferrest fro luste mynde worlde hole hole bren̄yng ye loue god whether prayenge thynkyng stylnes spekynge redyng herynge on̄lynes comonyng goynge syttyng kepe tyme werche therin allonge sauour lastyth yt thou take therwith mete drynke slepe pylgryme doth kepe discrecōn thy worchyng coūseyle ordynaūce ye soueryne haue neuer grete hast goynge yet wol ete drynke slepe thou lyke wyse though let one tyme shal forther nother tyme ¶of euyl daye gode nyghte meaneth ye loue worlde lykened euyl day loue god good nyght caplm̄ xxiiii yf thou wolt wyte desyre sothly ihū makyth desyre ye yeueth ye ye desyreth ī ye yt desyred al doth al yf thou myght see hym thou doost nought suffrest hym worche thy soule assentyst hym grete gladnesse herte yt wouche sauf thou arte nought elles resonable instrument wherin yt worcheth therfore whan thou felyst thy thought wehynge grace take vp desyre ihū myghty deuout wyl plese hȳ loue hȳ thē thynke yt thou hast ihū yt thou desyrest beholde hȳ wel goth yt ī bodely lyknes vnsēseably priue presē ce myght therfore see hym ghostly yf thou may festen althy thought thyn affeccyon hym folowe hym soo gooth shal lede ye ryght waye ihr̄lm syght pee contemplacyon thus prayed prophete fader heuē sayenge thus p xlii emitte lucē tuā veritatē tuam ipa deduxetunt et adduxetunt montemscm̄ tuū et tabernacula tua fader heuen sende thy lyght thy sothfastnesse yt thy sonne ihū anb shal lede desyre ye holy hylle thy tabernacle felynge perfyte loue heyght contēplacyon desyre speketh prophete thynkynges prophete sayth hath desyred god al ye nyght tymful space bytwyx dayes two whan one daye ended nother comyth anone fyrst comyth nyght departeth dayes somtyme longe somtyme shorte thenne comyth nother day prophete meaned on̄ly maner nyght meaned ghostly nyght thou shalt vnderstonde ben two dayes two lyghtes fyrste fals lyght • ecōde true lyght fals lyght loue worlde man hathe hymselfe corrupcyon hys flesshe true lyght perfyte loue ihesu felyd thorugh grace mannes soule loue worlde false lyght passeth awaye lasteth perfourmeth behoteth lyght behyght fende adam whan styre hym synne sayd thus gen̄ 3 aperientur oculus vestri et eritis sicut dii eyen shal opened ye shal goddys sayd sothe whan adā synned anone inner eye sperred ghostly lyght withdrawe vtter eye opened lyghte euerlastyngr saynt iohn̄ sayth qui diligit deum manet lumine isp̄ ioh • loueth god dwellyth lyght man perceyueth seeth lone worlde fals faylynge woll forsake seke loue ihesu maye assone fele loue hym muste abyde whyle nyghte maye sodeynly come fro one lyghte loue worlde perfyte loue god nyghte noughte elles forberynge withdrawynge thoughte soule fro erthly thynges grete desyre yernynge loue see fele ihesu gholy thynges nyght ryght nyght derke euer hydyng al bodely creature restynges bodely dedes ryght soo man settyth hym fully thynke ihesu desyre ye loue hym besye hyde thought fro vayne beholdynge perceyuynge affeccyon fro flesshly lykyng louynge al bodely creature thonght maye made free subget ne affeccyon bounde ne pyned ne troubled thynge lower ne woors selfe yf maye nyghte hym derknesse good nyght lyght derknesse stoppyng fals loue worlde nyghynge true daye sothly ye derker yt nyȝt ye nerer ye true daye loue ihū ye soule maye thorugh longyng god hydde fro noyse dyn̄e flesshly affeccyons vnclene thoughtes nerer fele lyght ye loue hym euen thus semyth prophete meaned whan sayd thus cū tenebris sedeo dn̄s lux mea est whan sitte derknes lorde lyght whā soule hydde fro styrynges syn̄e slepe lorde lyght then̄e nygheth grace shewe lyght neuertheles nyght somtyme paynfull fyrste whan man moche foule thorugh grace vsed often derknes wolde fayne haue therfore setteth thought desyre god warde asmoche maye wolde fele ne thynke on̄ly hym cause yt may lyghtly haue therfore paynfull custome homelynes hath synnes worlde flesshly affeccyons erthly thynges flesshly dedes prees vpon hym euer smite maystry draw downe soule hē may wel hidde fro hē assone wolde therfore derkenes paynful hym namly whan grace wchyth habundantly neuertheles yf heuy ne stryue moche though thou woldest thrugh maystry put hē oute thy thoughte thou maye doo soo abyde grace suffre easely breke thy self tomoche slyely yf thou maye drawe thy desyre thy glostly beholdyng ihū yf tho woldest charge hem wyte thou well whan thou woldest desire ihesu oonly thynke thou may frely prechyng suche worldly thoughtes sothly thon art outwarde fals day thou art entrīg derkenes thy derkenes restfull cause disease vncūnyng vnclennes thyself therfore vse ofte shal processe thrugh felinge grace easy restful whan thy soule thrugh grace made soo free soo myghty soo good gadred lyste thynke right noughte then̄e good derknesse nought meane thꝰ soule may thorugh gracebe gadred freely hooly driuen ayenst wyll ne drawē downe maystry thynke lyke loue wyth cleuīge affeccōn ony synne ol vaynly ony erthly thynge thēne thynketh soule nouȝt thē thynkith none erthly thyng cleuyngly ryche nought nought nyght grete ease ye soule yt desyreth ye loue ihesu ease thoughte ony erthly thynge neuertheles full besy thīke hym thynge makyth derkenes sothly noughte elles gracyous desyre haue loue ihū ye desyre ye longyng hath tyme ye loue god see hym haue hym dryueth oute herte al worldly vanytees flesshly affeccyons gadreth soule occupyeth oonly thynke myght come ye loue hym ye tyme maye freely deuoutly beholde ihū whed wol pray thinke bryngyth ryght nouȝt sothly al derke ne nouȝt whā thynkyth thꝰ though derke fro fals lyȝt al derke fro ye true lyȝt ihū yt loue lyȝt derknes wheder paynful restful paynful then̄e ye soule traueylyng desyre lōgyng lyght yet • restynge loue ne shewynge lyght therfore called nyghte derknesse asmoche soule hyd fro fals lyghte worlde hathe yet fully felynge true lighte abidyng blessid loue god whiche desyreth thene yf thou wolte wyte whan thou atte syker derkenesse whan thou may assay thꝰ seke ferder thus whan thou felyst thyn entente thy wyll fully sette desyre god thynke on̄ly hym thou maye fyrste aske thyself thyn owne thought whether thou coueyte haue ony thyng lyfe loue itselfe haue vse ony thy bodily wyttes ony creature thēne yf thyn eye āswere thꝰ wolde se right nought thy mouche wolde sauour right nonght thyn eere wolde ryght nought thy body wolde fele right nouȝt yf thine herte say wold thynke right nought erthly thynge ne bodily dede ne wolde haue affeccōn fastyned flesshly creature oonly ī god god warde yf yt cowde whā answere al thꝰ done ful redily yf grace towche then̄e art thou entred sō derknes though thou fele perceyue glētynges proferynges vayne thouȝtes presing flesshly affeccyons neuertheles thou art profitable derknes yt thy thought fyxed hē suche vayne ymagynacōns yt fal ye herte vnauysedly trowblē derknes pyneth ye soule sō cause yt wolde hyd fro hem may awaye ye profyte derknes soule shal ye way come restful myrknes derknes restful whan ye soule hyd tyme fro ye paynful felynge al suche vayn thouȝte • rested desyre lōginge ihū ghostly beholdyng hym shal sayd afterwarde ye lasteth whyle hole neuertheles though shorte tyme ful profytable ¶how yt desyre ihesu fele lyghtsom derknes sleeth al styrynges synne ableth soule perceyue ghostly lyghtynges fro heuenly iherusalem yt ihesu caplm̄ xxv sithen derknes nyght good restfull though shorte stondeth desyre longyng loue ihesu wyth blynde thynkynge hym good thenne blessyd fele loue illumided wyth blessyd vnseable present lyght see sothfastnes whiche lyght soule receyueth whā nyghte passith daye spryngeth hope nyght yt prophete meaned whan sayd soule hath desyred yt ye nyȝt haue sayd moche better hyd ī derke nyght fro beholdyng y• worlde though paynfull fals lykyng worlde yt semyth shinyng cōfortable hem yt blynde knowyng ghostly lyght whā thou art derknes thou art mekyl nerer ihr̄lm whan thou art myddes fals lyght therfore applye thyn herte fully steryng grace vse dwellen derknes often assayenge bē homely • shal sone made restful ye true lyght ghostly knowyng shal sprynge onys preuyly lytyl lytyl ye prophete sayth hītantibus regione vmbre marti lux orta est eis isisay ꝯ dwellyng countre shadowe deth lyght sprongen yt lyght grace spronge shal spryng al hem yt dwelle shadowe deth yt derknes yt lyke deth deth sleeth lyuyng body al flesshly felynges ryght desyre loue ihū felyd derkenes sleeth al synnes al flesshly affeccyons al vnclene thoughtes ye tyme nyghest thou fast ihr̄lm thou art yet smale sodeyne lyghtynges glydern outthorughe smale cauys fro cyte shalt thou mow seen fro ferre thou come therto wete thou well though thy soule restful derknes withouten troublyng worldly vanytees yet sholde yet clothyd al lyght ne turned al fyre loue felyth wel som aboue yt knowith ne hath yet wolde haue breunyngly desyreth elles lyght ihr̄lm without forth whiche lyke cyte prophete ezechyel sawe vysyons sayth sawe cyte sette vpon hylle heldynge ye south yt syght whan meten length brede rodde yt syxe cubytes palme lengthe sone brought cyte loked aboute hym thought hym yt wo • der mekyl sawe many halle chaumbrys open preuy sawe gate porch vtterwarde innerwarde mekyl byggyng saye length brede many hūdred cubytes thanne wonder hym cyte within longe large yt lytyl syght whan without length vi cubytes vnderstōde ye perfeccyon man̄es werke y• palme lytyl towchynge contēplacyon seeth well yt suche thynge yt passeth ye deserte al ye worchyng man lytyl palme passeth vi cubites seeth within neuertheles yf maye come within cyte contemplocyon thenne seeth moche sawe fyrste ¶how man shal knowe fals illumynacyons feyned fende fro ye true lyght knowynge ye comyth ihū token caplm̄ xxvi bewaar myddaye fende y• feyneth lyght came ihr̄lm ten • e seeth yt lorde ihū shewyth lyght louers sothfastnesse therfore • eceyuing hē yt vnwyse shewyth lyght yt true vnder colour true lyght deceyueth hē neuertheles soule may knowe lyght sothfastnes whan shyneth frō god whan feyned thorugh ye enmye shal saye thynketh ensample fyrmament somtym̄ fyrmament shewyth lyght fro sonne semyth ye sonne sōtyme shewyth ye true sonne truely knowing ye one ye feyned sonne wyth hym bitwixe two blacke reyny clowdes then̄e cause ye sonne nere shyneth fro clowles lyghte alōne none true sonne whan frymament clere moche clered fro blacke clowdes purpose mē semich forsakith loue worlde wold come loue god ye lyghte vnderstondynge hym woll come thrugh derknes haue spokē woll knowe hemfelfe truely ne mekely haue bē ne yet thrugh syn̄e ne nought owne kynde ayēst god besy entree hemself al thynges outwarde left flee al wicked stirynges yt rysen hertes pryde enuy yre synnes thrugh lastyng desyre ihesu prayēge thynkynge scylence wepynge bodily ghlostly exercyse deuoutemen holy men haue done assone haue forsake worlde outwarde lyknesse elles sone wene holy able haue ghostly vnderstondynge gospell holy wrytte namly yf maye fulfill letterly cōmaundementes god kepe hem fro bodily synnes wene yt loue god perfytly therfore wol anone preche teche al men yf receyued grace vnderstōdinge ī perfeccōn charyte thrugh specyall yeft holy ghost also ther moche styred moche fele somtyme moche knowyng sondenly yeuen hem wythout grete studye also moche feruour loue semyth preche trouth riȝtwysnes euēcrystē therfore holde grace god yt vylyteth hem blessid lyghte soules neuertheles yf wol loke wel aboute hem shal fynde yt lyght knowynge yt hete yt fele comith ye true son y• lorde ihū comyth fro y• myddaye fende yt feyneth lyght lykneth hym son therfore shal knowē example sayd lyght cūnyng y• feyned ye fende derke swole shewed bytwyx two blacke reyny clowdes ouer cloude presūpcyō hygheng hēself nether clowde downe puttyng aloweng enencrystē lyght knowyng felyng feruour y• y• shyneth soule wich presūpcyō hyȝeng disdeyne euencrystē y• tyme felyd lyght grace yeuen ye holy ghost though ye knowynge sothfast eyther fende yf come sodenly elles mannes owne wytte yf come studye may wel knowen yt feyned lyght knowyng y• lyght ye true son therfore y• haue knowyng maner ful ghostly pryde seen blynde feyned lyȝt yt holde ye highnes hert thū buxōnes ye lawes holy chyrche perfyte mekenes y• gospel lawes god wene folowyng owne wyl freedom spryte therfore begyn thapostle sayth thus uhi enim zelus et contencio ibi inconstā cia et omne opus prauum non est sapiencia hec desursū descēdens patre luminū sed est terrena īalis diabolica soo enuye flytynge vnstablynes euyll werke therfore cnnnynge bryngeth forth suche sīnes comyth frō sader lyghte good erthly beestly fendly thise tokēs pryde presūpcion vnbuxomnes indignacyon bacbytynge suche synnes conscyence made clene thrugh fyre brennyng desyre ihesu derkenes whyche wasteth brenneth alle wycked stirynges pryde vaynglory yre enuye al synnes soule prophete sayth ignis ante ipsū precedet et inflam mabit incircuitu iuimicos eiusp̄ ꝯꝯ fyre shal goo hym desyre loue shal go ihesu mā ne soule shal brēne enmyes shall waste synes yf soule fyrst smyten downe fro heighte itselfe drede mekenes purifyed made subtyll thorugh thys fyre thenne maye receyue gracyous lyght ghostly knowynge perfeccyō loue true sonne thus sayth holy wryte mō liiii uobis qui timetis deū oriet • ol iusticie ye true sonne rightwysnes yt lorde ihesu shal sprynge yo • dredē hym y• meke soules y• meken hemsel vnder euencristen knowīge owne wretchydnesse castē hēself downe wnder god noughtynge hemselfe owne substaunce thorugh reuerence drede ghostly beholdyng hym lastyngly perfyte mekenes unto thyse soules true son shal spryng illumyn reason knowynge sothfastnes kyndleth affeccyon brynnynge loue thenne shal bothe brenne shyne shall thorughe vertue heuenly sonne brenne perfyte loue shyne knowyng god ghostly thynges ben refourmed felynge therfore wol deceyued hope good hym drawe downe hymselfe hyde hym derkenes fyrst entermetyng mē haue sayd forgete worlde yf maye folowe ihesu lastynge desyre offered prayer thynkynge hym thenne trowe lyght comyth derkenes syker sothtaste shyneth cyte iherusalem true sonne soule traueyleth derknes cryeth lyght wyssen waye▪ comforte traueyle hope true derkenes comyth neuer teyned lyghte yf man truely fully sette hym forsake loue worlde maye thorughe grace come felynge knowynge hymselfe holde hym mekely felynge shall dysceyued wyth none erroures ne heresyes ne fantasyes alle thyse comen gate pryde thenne yf pryde may stopped thenne shal suche syn̄e rest soule thoughe come profer hem hem shall entre grace soule felyth meke derkenes shall teche soule sothtastnes shewe hym suche profetynges • enmyes ¶how grete profyte soule brought thorugh grace lyghtsom derknes man shall dyspose hym yf wol come therto caplm̄ xxvii many deuout soules thorugh grace come derkenes felen knowynge hemself yet wote fully ye vnknowynge partye hyndred hem fele wel often thought aff • ccyon drawen departed fro mynde erthly thynges brought grete rest delectable softnes without pinful trowblyng vayne thoughtes bodely wyttes fele ye tyme grete freedom spyryte yt maye thynke jhesu peasyble offre psalmes prayer myghtyly sauourly swetly hym aslonge freelte bodely kynde maye suffre wote wel yt felynge good noot therfore vnto suche soules saye thynketh yt maner felynge though shorte syldom soth fastly derkenes speke felyng hymselfe fyrst rysynge aboue hemselfe thorughe breunynge dysyre syght ihū elles yf shal saye sothly gracyous felynge ghostly syght ihesu yf maye kepe hem rest brynge thorughe grace custome yt myȝt lghtly freely haue whan hem lyst holde hem sholde neuer ouercome tēptycyon fende ne flesshe ne errours ne heresyes sette gate contemplacyon able redy receyue yt perfyte loue ihū therfore hath good yt knowe mekely kepe tenderly pursew feruently yt creature lette hym vtterly yt ne folowe whan maye yt forgete sette nought al thynge yt sholde put hym fro yf free hymself may wol without sclaunder dysease euencrystē thynkyth may come rest lyghtly haue grete plēte grace sette hym folowe ye styryng grace yt oweth grace wol euer free namely fro synne worldly besenes al thynges yt letten worthyng though synne neuertheles nother soule yt hath yet receyued fulnes grace yf desyre com̄ thꝭ ghostly knowyng ihū moche hym must able hym self put away al lettynges yt stoppen grace moche maye muste lerne deye ye worlde forsake ye loue truely fyrst pryde bodely ghostly yt desyre worthyp worldly cunnynge ne worldly cratt benefyces ne rychesse precyous clothīg ne worldely araye ne thynge thrugh sholde worshypes aboue mē shal coueyte none thise yf ben put vpon hym take hem drede yt poore outwarde warde elles fully inwarde herte yt coueyte forgetē ye worlde ye men rewarde hym neuer ryche ne cunnynge ye poorest man lyueth also suffreth herte reste beholding owne dedes vertues wenynge dooth better nother forsakyth worlde done therfore setteth wel hym selfe also muste leue rysynge herte euyll wyll yre enuye ayenst euencristen dysease noo man ne anger hym vnskyfully worde ne dede ne yeue ony man matere thorugh myghte skylfully angred styred soo mygh free fro euery man also forsake couetyse coueyte ryght noughte erthly goo • oonly aske bodely sustenaunce hym nedeth holde hym payd whan god styreth men yeue hym yt put manere truste hauour ony worldly good ne helpe fauour ony worldly frende pryncypally fully god yf doo otherwyse byndeth hymselfe worlde maye therfore free thynke ihesu also glotenye lecherye al flesshly vnclennes vtterly muste leue affeccyon bounde woman flesshly homlynesse dowte suche blynde loue somtyme atwyxe mā woman semyth good honest moche wolde notsynne dede syght god ful vnclene wel grete synne grete synne man shal suffre affeccyon sholde festened ihesu al vertues al ghostly clen̄es bounde ony flesshly loue ony creature wylfully namly yf moche bereth downe thoughte makyth vnrestfull maye sauour haue god thus holde wylfully man dooth sayth synne elles blynded woll see also man coueyte delyces mete drynkes oonly luste flesshe holde hym payd suche mete may easely haue therfore myght come therto muste thyse saīt poul dide sayēg thꝰ michi mundus crucifixus est et ego mūdo worlde slayne crucyfied gal v worlde yt hath forsake loue worlde worshippes rich worldly thynges sayd loue god loueth ne pursewyth well payd hathe right nought ne wolde haue though myghte sothly hym worlde dede hath noo sauour ne delyte theryn also yf worlde sette hym nought hath noo rewarde hym ne fauour ne worshyp ne sette noo pryce hym forgeteth hym dede man thenne dede worlde plyght saynt poul sette perfytly soo must nother mā partye wolde folowe come perfite loue god may lyue god fully yf deye fyrst worlde deyenge worlde derkenes gate cōtemplacōn refourmyng felyng none may many sūdryd wayes seere werkes lettinge ledyng sūdry soulys contēplacion diuers disposynges men sundry state religyous seculers dyuers exercise worchyng neuertheles noo gate one exercise soule hath yf maye come exercyse knowyng meke felynge hymself mortifyed dede worlde loue maye fele hymself somtyme restful derkenes whiche maye hydde fro vanytee worlde loue maye fele hymselfe sothly yet come refourmynge felynge ne hath fully contemplaciō ful ferre therfro yf woll come gate theyf wyl grace worcheth maner wyse doth ro viii saynt poul reherceth thus quos deus p̄scinit fieri conformes ymaginis filii eius ho vocauit et quos vocauit ho iustificauit et quos iustificauit ho magnificauit et quos magnificauit ho et glorificabit thise ye god knewe sholde made shapely ymage sonne thyse called thyse ryghted thyse magnyfyed thyse gloryfyed though thyse wordes maye sayd chosen soules lowest degre charyte refourmed on̄ly fayth neuertheles may vnderstonde specyally thyse soules arne refourmed felynge whiche lorde god shewyth moche plente grace doth moche besynes aboute hem owne sone specyally fulshappe lyckenes sonne ihū whiche wordes saynt poule departeth worchyng lorde foure tymes fyrst tyme callynge soule fro worldly vanyte tyme often easy comfortable begynnynge tornynge suche man disposed moche grace soo quyckely felyngly inspyred felyth oft grete swetnes deuocion hath many teres compunction y• thynkyth hym somtyme halfe henen softnes passyth tyme thēne comyth seconde tyme tyme ryghtynge yt trauelous whan begynneth goo forth myghtely waye ryghtwysnes settyth wylful ayenst al synne without within stretchith desyre vertues loue ihū thenne felyth moche truste lorde leueth suche soule goo neuer soo ferre fro whyche soule borne vp fro dispeyre saued fro ghostly myscheyf also wythout itselfe shal mortifyed pyned sēsualyte eyther dyuers syknes feable tourment fende elles thrugh preuy myghte god sely soule felynge berynge wretched body shal soo pyned shal wyte shall mow suffre bo • ne lorde ihesu kept therin yet neuertheles soule leuer alle pyne blinded wyth fals loue worlde helle suche soule sufferynge manere pyne noughte purgatory therfore suffryth gladly wolde putte awaye though myghte soo prouffytable dooth oure lorde grete prouffyte soule dryue oute sēsualyte myghte receyue ghostly lyghte whan soule thus mortyfied brought fro worldly loue derknesse yt hathe noo sauour ne delyte worldly lykynge ye strawe thynkye bytter wormode thenne commyth thirde tyme magnyfieng whan soule refourmed felynge partye receyueth yefte perfeccyon grace contemplacyon tyme grete reste thenne ihesu homely soule comyth fourth tyme gloryfyenge whan soule shall fully refourmed blysse heuen thyse soules arne thus called fro synne thus ryghted elles maner lyke dyuers assayenge bothe thoroughe fyre water afterwarde thus magnyfyed sholde gloryfyed rightyng way lorde sayth prophete worde grete confort suche soules examined wyth fyre tribulacyon thus puer meus noli timereisa xliii si transieris perignem flamma non nocebitte chylde yf thou passe thorugh fyre drede flame shal deere shall clēse fro flesshly fylthe make able receyue ghostly fyre loue god nedeth done fyrst haue sayd maye elles refourmed felynge ¶how falleth somtyme soules begyn̄yng profytynge grace seme haue loue outwarde tokēs haue ben perfyte yet soo soth wythin caplm̄ xxix sayest thou maye sothe many soules newe tourned god haue many ghostly felynges haue grete compunction synnes haue grete deuocyons feruours prayer often haue sundry techinges ghostly liȝte vnderstonding men haue maner felynges confortable hete grete swetnes neuertheles thise soules come sothfast gracyously yeuē god thyse soules felen suche yet refourmed felynge ne haue yet y• yefte perfecciō ne ghostly brenninge loue ihū maye come neuertheles often semyth otherwyse suche soules fele loue god thā haue yefte perfeccyon asmoche felyng shewyth outwarde grete feruour bodily token wepynge prayenge knelinge spekynge bodily styrynge soo ferforth semyth nother man euer rauysshed loue though thynkith soo wel wote thise maner felinges feruours deuociō compunccion thise men fele gracious • eftes god sent chosē soules drawe hē worldly loue flesshly luste hath ben longe tyme roted hert fro whiche loue sholde drawē bi suche feable stirynge grete feruours neuer theles yt feruours somoche outwarde shewyng on̄ly mochenes loue yt haue litylnes weyknes soule may bere lityl yt hath gretly defoylled syn̄e shal refourmed felynge yf fyrste brente purifyed wyth suche grete compunccyons goynge another soule neuer moche defoyleth wyth loue ye worlde hath euer kepte fro grete synnes innocēce maye lyghtlyer pryuely wythout grete feruour shewed outwarde com̄ refourmynge thenne soch hope suche comfortes feruours soule felyth state begyn̄ynge profytyng ghostly foode sente fro gadred ī departed fro beholdynge al erthly thynges fro vse bodely wittes felyth owne kynde without body thenne yf thou coueyte knowe see thy soule thou shalte torne thy thought ymaginacion thy body
